function checkhead2() { //check:通過前
	var Nmday="20260126";
	var Nm3day = "";
	if (document.all("txtspecdt").value != '') {
		if (checkdate(1,document.all("txtspecdt").value) == false){
			return false;
			}
		if (Nmday==''){
			alert('今日日期不正確');
			return false;
			}		
		if (Nmday>document.all("txtspecdt").value){
			alert('指定特殊付款日不可小於今日' + Nmday);
			return false;
			}	

		if ( ('1' == "5") ){
			if (Nmday==document.all("txtspecdt").value){
				alert('指定特殊付款日不可等於今日' + Nmday);
				return false;
				}	
		    }			
	}
}
	
function checkhead() { //check:送件者送出及決裁者送出	

	//if  ( ('1' != "5") && (document.frmbdy.SELTOCOMP.value !="5") ){
		if  (document.frmbdy.CLTEL.value == ''){
			alert('連絡電話不可空白');
			document.frmbdy.CLTEL.focus();
			return false;
			}
		if  (document.frmbdy.CLCREATER.value == ''){
			alert('發行人不可空白');
			document.frmbdy.CLTEL.focus();
			return false;
			}
	//if  ( (document.frmbdy.ActCenterName.value !="集約") && (document.frmbdy.SELTOCOMP.value !="5") ){
	if  ((document.frmbdy.SELTOCOMP.value !="5") || (document.frmbdy.ActCenterName.value =="集約")){
		var togln = document.frmbdy.tog.length;
		var flow1cntto = 0;
		for (icount=togln-1;icount>0;icount--){
			if  (document.frmbdy.tog[icount].value == '0'){
				if (document.frmbdy.hdMANNO.value != document.frmbdy.to[icount].value){
					//window.alert(document.frmbdy.ton[icount].value);
					flow1cntto = flow1cntto +1;
					} else {
					//window.alert(document.frmbdy.ton[icount].value);
					flow1cntto = 0;
					}
				}
			}			
		//支付對象以外只有一個
		//window.alert(document.frmbdy.ActCenterName.value);
		if(flow1cntto <= 0 && document.frmbdy.STFLSTATUS.value != "4") {
			alert('請求付款書的支付對象,需要上一階主管確認!\n(流程異動請聯絡iEPOCH擔當)');
			return false;
			}
		//return false;
	}
	if(document.frmbdy.txtyear.value=='' || document.frmbdy.txtmon.value=='' || document.frmbdy.txtday.value==''){
		alert('申請日不可空白,請重開畫面!');
		document.frmbdy.txtyear.focus();
		document.frmbdy.scrollIntoView();
		return false;	
		}
	if ( ('1' == "5") ){
		if (document.frmbdy.txtyear.value+ document.frmbdy.txtmon.value+document.frmbdy.txtday.value==document.all("txtspecdt").value){
			alert('指定特殊付款日不可等於今日:' + document.frmbdy.txtyear.value+ document.frmbdy.txtmon.value+document.frmbdy.txtday.value);
			return false;
			}	
		}
	if(document.frmbdy.oRowcnt.value=='' || document.frmbdy.oRowcnt.value=='0'){
		alert('請輸入資料');
		return false;	
		}
	if 	(document.frmbdy.hdMANNO.value == ''){
		alert('受款人代號不可空白');
		document.frmbdy.hdMANNO.focus();
		return false;
		}
	if 	(document.frmbdy.hdAMT.value != '' || document.frmbdy.hdTMPNO.value != ''){
		if 	(document.frmbdy.hdAMT.value == ''){
			alert('沖暫借款金額不可空白');
			document.frmbdy.hdTMPNO.focus();
			return false;
			}
		if 	(document.frmbdy.hdTMPNO.value == ''){
			alert('沖暫借款號碼不可空白');
			document.frmbdy.hdAMT.value = '';
			document.frmbdy.hdTMPNO.focus();
			return false;
			}
		}
		
	if	((document.frmbdy.hdAMT.value != document.frmbdy.RGMONEY.value) && (document.frmbdy.hdMANNA.value == '' || document.frmbdy.hdBankNo.value == '' || document.frmbdy.hdCountNo.value == '' || document.frmbdy.hdCrItmNo.value == '')){
		alert('沒有受款人電匯帳號,請重新輸入受款人代號.');
		document.frmbdy.hdMANNO.focus();
		return false;
		}

	if  (document.frmbdy.TotalC.value == ''){
		alert('借方科目金額不可空白');
		document.frmbdy.POBJNO.focus();
		return false;
		}

	if  (document.frmbdy.TotalC.value.length > 11){
		alert('科目總金額不可大於11位');
		return false;
		}
	
	var chktax1 = parseInt(DeAddCommaH(document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY.value),10);
	var chktax2 = parseInt(DeAddCommaH(document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY2.value),10);
	var chk1 = 0;
	var chkG = parseInt(DeAddCommaH(document.frmbdy.RGMONEY.value),10);
	var chkC = parseInt(DeAddCommaH(document.frmbdy.TotalC.value),10);
	
	if (document.frmbdy.hdAMT.value != ''){
		chk1 = parseInt(DeAddCommaH(document.frmbdy.hdAMT.value),10) ;
		if (chk1 > chkC){
			alert('沖暫借款不可大於總額.' + chkC);
			document.frmbdy.hdAMT.focus();
			return false;
			}
		}
	else if  (chkG <= 0){ //20121212
		alert('付款傳票的給付淨額需要大於零.');
		document.frmbdy.RGMONEY.select();
		document.frmbdy.RGMONEY.focus();
		return false;
		}
	
	chkA = chk1 + chkG + chktax1 + chktax2;
	if  (chkA != chkC){
		alert('金額借' + chkC + '貸' + chkA + '不相等.');
		document.frmbdy.RGMONEY.select();
		document.frmbdy.RGMONEY.focus();
		return false;
		}
		
	//20190502	
	tot = 0;
	nettot = 0;
	creadv_tot = 0;
	renhiamt_tot=0;
	hdVHRCNT = parseInt(window.parent.mail.frmbdy['hdVHRCNT'].value,10);
	//renhiamt

	for (xx = 1; xx <= hdVHRCNT; xx++){
		if (document.all['retotrat'+xx].value != ''){
			tot = tot + parseFloat(DeAddCommaH(document.all['retotrat'+xx].value));
			}
		if (document.all['renhirat'+xx].value != ''){
			nettot = nettot + parseFloat(DeAddCommaH(document.all['renhirat'+xx].value));
			}

		if (document.all['retotamt'+xx].value != ''){
			creadv_tot = creadv_tot + parseFloat(DeAddCommaH(document.all['retotamt'+xx].value));
			}

		if (document.all['renhiamt'+xx].value != ''){
			renhiamt_tot = renhiamt_tot + parseFloat(DeAddCommaH(document.all['renhiamt'+xx].value));
			}		
		}
	
	if (tot<0){
		window.alert("所得通報資料的扣繳稅額合計,必需大於零.");
		return false;
		}
	if (document.frmbdy.SELTOCOMP.value !="5" && document.frmbdy.A33item.value !="11"){

		if (DeAddCommaH(window.parent.mail.frmbdy.TAXMONEY.value) != tot){
			alert("所得通報資料的[扣繳稅額 $"+tot+"]和[稅款代扣金額$"+DeAddCommaH(window.parent.mail.frmbdy.TAXMONEY.value)+"]不相等.")
			return false;
			}

		if (DeAddCommaH(window.parent.mail.frmbdy.TAXMONEY2.value) !=nettot){
			alert("所得通報資料的[健保扣費$"+nettot+"]和[健保代扣$"+window.parent.mail.frmbdy.TAXMONEY2.value+"]金額不相等.")
			 return false;
			}	
		//20191202
		if (renhiamt_tot >creadv_tot){
			alert("所得通報資料的[給付淨額$"+renhiamt_tot+"]大於[給付總額$"+creadv_tot+"].")
			return false;
			}		
			
	}		
		
	return true;
}

function btnf_onclick_step2(strtmp1,sign,imgname,username,mlevel,spnplace,imgplace) {
    if (typeof (strtmp1) == "undefined")
        return;
    if (strtmp1.substring(4, 5) != "+")
        return;
    strtmp1 = unescape(strtmp1);
    strtmp = strtmp1.substring(0, 4);
    document.frmbdy.formsend.value = strtmp;
    //alert(strtmp1.substring(5,strtmp1.length));   

    document.all("flow_STFLMEMO").value = strtmp1.substring(5, strtmp1.length);
    if (document.all("flow_STFLMEMO").value != "") {
        document.all("flow_STFLMEMO_table1").style.display = "";
        document.all("flow_STFLMEMO_name").innerText = username + ":";
        document.all("flow_STFLMEMO").style.display = "";
    }
    else {
        document.all("flow_STFLMEMO_table1").style.display = "none";
    }
    // alert(document.all("flow_STFLMEMO").value);
    //alert(strtmp);

	switch (strtmp){
		case "pass":			
			impress_onclick(imgname,username,mlevel,spnplace,imgplace,'','');
			document.frmbdy.STFLSTATUS.value = "3";
			document.frmbdy.STFLKEEP.value = "N";
			document.frmbdy.btnsend.disabled = false;
		if (checkare() == false){  //20180515
			alert("不可輸入 '=' ,'~','^','&' 等特殊符號! ");
			return;
			}
	 
            document.frmbdy.btnsend.style.color = "green"
			chkspnplace = "";
			document.frmbdy.btnsend.focus();
			break;
		case "reje":
			pmt = username + "不通過";
			document.all(spnplace).innerHTML = "<font color=red size=2><TEXTAREA readonly rows=3 cols=12 id=are" + spnplace + " name=are" + spnplace + ">" + pmt + "</TEXTAREA></font>";
			document.frmbdy.STFLSTATUS.value = "4";
			document.frmbdy.STFLKEEP.value = "N";
			document.frmbdy.btnsend.disabled = false;
            document.frmbdy.btnsend.style.color = "green"
  		if (document.all("date"+spnplace)!=null){//決裁日期
            document.all("date"+spnplace).innerHTML  = "<font color=red size=1></font>";//clear date 20180615
		}
			chkspnplace = spnplace;
			document.all("are"+chkspnplace).focus();
			break;
		case "keep":
			pmt = username + "保留";
			document.all(spnplace).innerHTML = "<font color=red size=2><TEXTAREA readonly rows=3 cols=12 id=are" + spnplace + " name=are" + spnplace + ">" + pmt + "</TEXTAREA></font>";
			document.frmbdy.STFLSTATUS.value = "2";
			document.frmbdy.STFLKEEP.value = "Y";
			document.frmbdy.btnsend.disabled = false;
            document.frmbdy.btnsend.style.color = "green"
		if (document.all("date"+spnplace)!=null){//決裁日期
            document.all("date"+spnplace).innerHTML  = "<font color=red size=1></font>";//clear date 20180615
		}
			chkspnplace = spnplace;
			document.all("are"+chkspnplace).focus();
			break;
		default:
			return;
		}
}

//載入印章:1.已決信件impress_restore;2.目前未決btnf_onclick
function impress_onclick(imgname,username,mlevel,spnplace,imgplace,agntname,seq) {	
/*alert('imgname: '+ imgname); 
alert('username: '+ username); 
alert('mlevel: '+ mlevel); 
alert('spnplace: '+ spnplace); 
alert('imgplace: '+ imgplace); 
alert('agntname: '+ agntname); 
alert('seq: '+ seq); */

	if(''=="T"){
		if (typeof impress_onclick_check === "function") {
			if (impress_onclick_check() === true) {
				// 執行
			} else {
				return;
			}
		} else {
		
		}
	}

 var date1;
    var date_tod;
    var d = new Date();	
    var yyyy=d.getFullYear();	//給定年變數並轉成西元年
    var mm = (d.getMonth()+1);	//給定月變數
    var dd = d.getDate();	//給定日變數
			//月、日轉2位數
     if (mm<10){
         mm = "0" + mm;
     } 
     if (dd<10){
        dd ="0" + dd;
     }
    date_tod = yyyy.toString()+mm.toString()+dd.toString();
    if ("Y"=="Y"){ 
        if ( seq == "" ) {
            date1 = date_tod;
            } //決裁           
        else if ( seq == "00" ) {
            //sender
            if (imgname == window.document.getElementById("from").value){
                date1 = window.document.getElementById("fromd").value;
                }          
            } else if ( seq >= "01" ) {
                if (window.document.getElementsByName("tod").length>1) 
                {
                    for (y=1;y<window.document.getElementsByName("tod").length;y++) {
   		                if (window.document.getElementsByName("to")[y].value==imgname && window.document.getElementsByName("toq")[y].value==seq)
                        {
		                    date1 = window.document.getElementsByName("tod")[y].value;
                        }
	                }//end of for
                }
           }
        } else {
           date1 = "";
        }

    if (spnplace == "spnfromi"){
		spnplace = "spnf" + document.getElementById("fromi").value;
    }
    if (document.all("date"+spnplace)!=null){//決裁日期
		document.all("date"+spnplace).innerHTML  = "<font color=red size=1>"+date1+"</font>";
    }
    //(結束) 顯示決裁日期 

    //(開始) 顯示代理章 
    var agent_st="";
    var agtstr="";

        if ( seq == "" ){
           //決裁
            if (window.document.getElementsByName("tod").length>1)	 {
                  for (y=1;y<window.document.getElementsByName("tod").length;y++) 	{
 			            if (window.document.getElementsByName("to")[y].value==imgname && ( window.document.getElementsByName("tos")[y].value==1  || window.document.getElementsByName("tos")[y].value==2))  {
			                var tmpstr=window.document.getElementsByName("ton")[y].value;
                            if (tmpstr.slice(-4)=="(代理)") {
		          	            agent_st="Y";
                            }	 
			            }
			        }
	        }                     
        }  

       if (agntname != "" || agent_st == "Y") {
           agtstr = "<img src='../SIGN/AGENT.bmp'>"; 
        }

    //(結束) 顯示代理章		
    //不通過時要處裡可能殘留的前一個"日期"及"代理章"資料	
	
	if ( date1 >= '20240805' ){	//20240805 全員刻章前文件維持不變
		//員工代號6 or 8碼、中文名字中沒有"["符號
		if ( (imgname.length==6 || imgname.length==8) && username.indexOf('[') == -1 ){
			//預先載入
			var img = new Image();
			img.src = "../SIGN/" + imgname + ".bmp";
			window.document.getElementById(spnplace).innerHTML="<font color=red size=2><img src='../SIGN/" + imgname + ".bmp'>" + agtstr + "</font><INPUT TYPE=HIDDEN id=hid" + spnplace + " name=hid" + spnplace + ">";
			}
		else{
			document.all(spnplace).innerHTML  = "<font color=red size=2>" + username + "通過" + agtstr + " </font><INPUT TYPE=HIDDEN id=hid" + spnplace + " name=hid" + spnplace + ">";
			} 	
	}else{
		if ( parseFloat(mlevel) > 5 ){
			//預先載入
			var img = new Image();
			img.src = "../SIGN/" + imgname + ".bmp";
			window.document.getElementById(spnplace).innerHTML="<font color=red size=2><img src='../SIGN/" + imgname + ".bmp'>" + agtstr + "</font><INPUT TYPE=HIDDEN id=hid" + spnplace + " name=hid" + spnplace + ">";
			}
		else{//level=5以下用姓名表示
			document.all(spnplace).innerHTML  = "<font color=red size=2>" + username + "通過" + agtstr + " </font><INPUT TYPE=HIDDEN id=hid" + spnplace + " name=hid" + spnplace + ">";
			} 
	}

}


//已存信件載入印章或評議
function impress_restore(st,imgname,username,mlevel,spnplace,imgplace,agntname,seq) {

	if (st == "3"){
		impress_onclick(imgname,username,mlevel,spnplace,imgplace,agntname,seq);
		document.all("flow_STFLMEMO").innerText = unescape("");//document.all(imgname).value
		}
    else if (st == "4"){
		document.all(spnplace).innerHTML ="<font color=red size=2>" + username + "不通過</font><INPUT TYPE=HIDDEN id=hid" + spnplace + " name=hid" + spnplace + ">";
		document.all("flow_STFLMEMO").innerText = unescape("");//document.all(imgname).value
		if (document.all("date"+spnplace)!=null){//決裁日期
		  document.all("date"+spnplace).innerHTML  = "<font color=red size=1></font>";//clear date 20180613
		}

        }
	else{
		//document.all(spnplace).innerHTML = "<font color=red size=2><TEXTAREA rows=3 cols=12 id=are" + spnplace + " name=are" + spnplace + " readonly>" + imgname + "</TEXTAREA></font>";
		//document.all("are" + spnplace).innerHTML ="<font color=red size=2>" + username + "不通過</font>";
		document.all(spnplace).innerHTML ="<font color=red size=2>" + "" + "</font><INPUT TYPE=HIDDEN id=hid" + spnplace + " name=hid" + spnplace + ">";
		document.all("flow_STFLMEMO").innerText = unescape("");//document.all(imgname).value;
		if (document.all("date"+spnplace)!=null){//決裁日期
		  document.all("date"+spnplace).innerHTML  = "<font color=red size=1></font>";//clear date 20180613
		}
}
}

//儲存前
function btnsave_onclick_check() {
    return true;
}

//儲存
function btnsave_onclick(rc) {

	if (rc == "upfile" || rc == "upfile2"){
	    if (btnsave_onclick_check()!=true)
		    return;

   		document.all("errmsg").innerText="";
		document.all("runmsg").innerText="訊息:儲存處理中,請稍候.";
	
		document.frmbdy.hidsubmit.value = "save";
		document.frmbdy.hidupfile.value = rc;
		document.frmbdy.submit();
		return;
		}
	
	if (rc == "True") {
		tmpstr = "已經儲存過,是否再存一次?";
		}
	else {
		tmpstr = "是否儲存?";
		}
	if (window.confirm(tmpstr)){
	    if (btnsave_onclick_check()!=true)
		    return;

		document.all("errmsg").innerText="";
		document.all("runmsg").innerText="訊息:儲存處理中,請稍候.";
	
		document.frmbdy.hidsubmit.value = "save";
		document.frmbdy.submit();
	}
}

//送出
function btnsend_onclick(DOCSTATUS) {	
	if (btnsend_onclick_check()!=true)
		return;
	
	document.frmbdy.btnsend.disabled = true;
	if (DOCSTATUS != "B"){
		//20081107
		if (document.frmbdy.flowcfm.value >= "1") {
			btnflshow_onclick(DOCSTATUS);
			}
		if (document.frmbdy.flowcfm.value >= "1"){
			window.alert("ERR" + document.frmbdy.flowcfm.value + ":" + "流程未確認,無法決裁!");
			document.frmbdy.btnsend.disabled = false;
			document.frmbdy.btnsend.style.color="green";
			return;
			}
		}
	if (chkspnplace.length == 5){
        //檢查是評語
		//if (checkare() == false){
			//alert("err");
			//return;
			//}
		}
		
	document.all("errmsg").innerText="";		
	document.all("runmsg").innerText="訊息:送出處理中,請稍候.";
	document.frmbdy.hidsubmit.value = "send";
	document.frmbdy.submit();
}

function checkare() {
	//inttmp = document.all("are"+chkspnplace).value.length ;
    strtmp = document.all("flow_STFLMEMO").value;
    strtmp1 = escape(document.all("flow_STFLMEMO").value);
    inttmp = strtmp.length ;
    inttmp1 = strtmp1.length ;

//----------------------------
 
 //alert(strtmp);
 var tmpChr
 for(var i=0;i<inttmp ;i++)
 {
  tmpChr = strtmp.substr(i,1);
  switch (tmpChr)
  {
   case '=':
     return false;
    break;
    case '~':
     return false;
    break;
    case '^':
     return false;
    break;
    case '&':
     return false;
    break;    
   default:
     
  }
 }

//----------------
	if (inttmp1 > 600){
		window.alert("對不起!!您的批註文字,不能超過100字!");
		return false;
		}
	return true;
}

//載入視窗事件
function window_onload() {
	try{
		parent.opener.parent.frames["main"].document.all("inopenwin").value -= -1;
		}
	catch(e){}
	document.all("runmsg").innerText="";
	show();
	
	window_onload_other();	
}

//釋放視窗事件
function window_onunload() {
	cnt_unload += 1;
	if (cnt_unload>1) {
		parent.opener.parent.frames["right"].location.reload();
		return;}
	try{
		parent.opener.parent.frames["main"].document.all("inopenwin").value -=  1;
		parent.opener.parent.frames["right"].location.reload();
		}
	catch(e){}
	
	window_onunload_other();
}

//關閉
function btnclose_onclick() {
	try{
		parent.opener.parent.frames["right"].location.reload();
		}
	catch(e){}
	parent.window.close(); 
}

var trncard = '001';
var CSTDYN  = '';
function AccPrint_onclick() {
	//document.all('errmsg').innerText='';
	document.all('errmsg').style.display = 'none';
	document.all('runmsg').style.display = 'none';
	//document.all('comptitle').innerText='';
	document.body.topMargin=10;
	frmbdy.btnflshow.style.display = 'none';
	frmbdy.ITMGET.style.display = 'none';
	frmbdy.BUGGET.style.display = 'none';
	frmbdy.SELGET.style.display = 'none';
	frmbdy.AccPrint.style.display = 'none';
	if (trncard == '001'){
		document.all.HDAccount.style.display = 'none';
		}
	else if (trncard == '002'){
		//document.all.HDAccount1.style.display = 'none';
		//document.all.HDAccount2.style.display = 'none';
		//document.all.HDAccount3.style.display = 'none';
		frmbdy.hdACCGET.style.display = 'none';
		frmbdy.hdExRate.style.display = 'none';
		//document.all.SPANhdExRate.style.display = 'none';
		}
	else if (trncard == '003'){
		document.all.HDAccount.style.display = 'none';
		frmbdy.btnvhr.style.display = 'none';
		}
	if (parent.frames['mail'].frmbdy.SELTOCOMP.value != '5'){
	document.all('idfirst').style.display = 'none';
	}
	
	document.all('FontDocno').color = 'black';
	document.all('FontAuto').color = 'black';
	document.all('trnkeyno').style.color = 'black';
	document.all('otbl').borderColor = 'black';
	document.all('otbl_net').borderColor = 'black';
	try{
	document.all('HDdatain').borderColor = 'black';
	document.all('hdBtnMemo').style.display = 'none';
	}
	catch(e){}
	try{
	document.all('vhrHDdatain').borderColor = 'black';
	document.all('btnvhr').style.display = 'none';
	}
	catch(e){}
	document.all('spanFormTitle').style.backgroundColor  = '';
	if (CSTDYN=='Y') {
		document.all('btnspecdt').style.border  = 'none';
		document.all('btnspecdt').style.backgroundColor  = 'white';
		document.all('btnspecdt').style.color  = 'black';
		document.all('btnspecdt').disabled  = false;
		}
	document.all('DAY_VHRNO').style.display = 'none';
	document.all('FONT3of9').style.display = 'none';
	window.print();
	window_onafterprint();
}

function window_onafterprint() {
	document.body.topMargin=10;
	document.all('errmsg').style.display = '';
	document.all('runmsg').style.display = '';
	//document.all('comptitle').innerText=document.frmbdy.txtmarea.value;
	frmbdy.btnflshow.style.display = '';
	frmbdy.ITMGET.style.display = '';
	frmbdy.BUGGET.style.display = '';
	frmbdy.SELGET.style.display = '';
	frmbdy.AccPrint.style.display = '';
	document.all('idfirst').style.display = '';
	if (trncard == '001'){
		document.all.HDAccount.style.display = '';
		}
	else if (trncard == '002'){
		//document.all.HDAccount1.style.display = '';
		//document.all.HDAccount2.style.display = '';
		//document.all.HDAccount3.style.display = '';
		frmbdy.hdACCGET.style.display = '';
		frmbdy.hdExRate.style.display = '';
		//document.all.SPANhdExRate.style.display = '';
		}
	else if (trncard == '003'){
		document.all.HDAccount.style.display = '';
		frmbdy.btnvhr.style.display = '';
		btnvhr_onclick('print');		
		}
	if (CSTDYN=='Y') {
		document.all('btnspecdt').style.border  = '';
		document.all('btnspecdt').style.backgroundColor  = '';
		document.all('btnspecdt').style.color  = '';
		document.all('btnspecdt').disabled  = true;
		}
	document.all('DAY_VHRNO').style.display = '';
	document.all('FONT3of9').style.display = '';
}

function old_btnf_onclick(sign,imgname,username,mlevel,spnplace,imgplace) {
	try{
		if (document.frmbdy['to'].length == 1){
			window.alert("對不起!!沒有流程,無法決裁!");
			document.frmbdy['btnsend'].disabled = true;
			document.frmbdy.btnsend.style.color = "silver"
			return;
			}
		if (sign == false){//寄件人不詢問
		    impress_onclick(imgname,username,mlevel,spnplace,imgplace,'','');//20180607
			//蓋章後才能送出
			document.frmbdy['btnsend'].disabled = false;
			document.frmbdy.btnsend.style.color = "green"
			return;
			}
		}catch(e){return;}		
	//alert(strtmp);
	//收件人詢問
	//strtmp = window.showModalDialog('peph1460.asp','pass','status:no;dialogWidth:250px;dialogHeight:200px;dialogLeft:200;dialogTop:110;help:no;resizable:yes');
	//20140305
	btnf_onclick_step1(sign,imgname,username,mlevel,spnplace,imgplace);
	}
//20140305	
function old_btnf_onclick_step2(strtmp,sign,imgname,username,mlevel,spnplace,imgplace) {
	//alert(strtmp);
	switch (strtmp){
		case 'pass':			
		    impress_onclick(imgname,username,mlevel,spnplace,imgplace,'','');//20180607
			document.frmbdy['STFLSTATUS'].value = "3";
			document.frmbdy['STFLKEEP'].value = "N";
			document.frmbdy['btnsend'].disabled = false;
			document.frmbdy.btnsend.style.color = "green"
			chkspnplace = "" //20001102 newchange
			document.frmbdy.btnsend.focus();
			break;
		case 'reject':
			pmt = username + '不通過';
			document.all(spnplace).innerHTML = '<font color=red size=2><TEXTAREA rows=4 cols=16 id=arespnf1 name=arespnf1>' + pmt + '</TEXTAREA></font>';
			document.frmbdy['STFLSTATUS'].value = "4";
			document.frmbdy['STFLKEEP'].value = "N";
			document.frmbdy['btnsend'].disabled = false;
			document.frmbdy.btnsend.style.color = "green"
			chkspnplace = 'spnf1';
			document.frmbdy['are'+chkspnplace].focus();
			break;
		case 'keep':
			pmt = username + '保留';
			document.all(spnplace).innerHTML = "<font color=red size=2><TEXTAREA rows=4 cols=16 id=arespnf1 name=arespnf1 >" + pmt + "</TEXTAREA></font>";
			document.frmbdy['STFLSTATUS'].value = "2";
			document.frmbdy['STFLKEEP'].value = "Y";
			document.frmbdy['btnsend'].disabled = false;
			document.frmbdy.btnsend.style.color = "green"
			chkspnplace = 'spnf1';
			document.frmbdy['are'+chkspnplace].focus();
			break;
		default:
			return;
		}		
}
var COMPANYID  = '';
//載入印章:1.已決信件impress_restore;2.目前未決btnf_onclick
function old_impress_onclick(imgname,username,mlevel,spnplace,imgplace,agntname,seq) {//20180607
    //2001/03/01
    /*
	if (spnplace == 'spnfromi'){
		spnplace = 'spnf' + document.all('fromi').value;
		}
	if (parseFloat(mlevel) > 5){
		document.all(spnplace).innerHTML = "<font color=red size=2><img src='../SIGN/" + imgname + ".bmp'></font><INPUT TYPE=HIDDEN id=hid" + spnplace + " name=hid" + spnplace + ">";
		}
	else{//20071226
		document.all(spnplace).innerHTML  = "<font color=red size=2>" + impress_trns(username) + "通過</font><INPUT TYPE=HIDDEN id=hid" + spnplace + " name=hid" + spnplace + ">";
		}
	*/
    //(開始)  顯示決裁日期 20180607
    var date1;
    var date_tod;
    var d = new Date();	
    var yyyy=d.getFullYear();	//給定年變數並轉成西元年
    var mm = (d.getMonth()+1);	//給定月變數
    var dd = d.getDate();	//給定日變數
    //月、日轉2位數
    if (mm<10){
        mm = '0' + mm;
    } 
    if (dd<10){
        dd = '0' + dd;
    }
    date_tod = yyyy.toString()+mm.toString()+dd.toString();
   
    if ('Y'=='Y')
    { 
        if ( seq == '' ) {date1 = date_tod;  } //決裁                           
        else if ( seq == '00' ) {
            //sender
            if (imgname == window.document.getElementById('from').value){date1 = window.document.getElementById('fromd').value;}          
        } 
        else if ( seq >= '01' ) {
            if (window.document.getElementsByName('tod').length>1)  {
                for (y=1;y<window.document.getElementsByName('tod').length;y++)  {
                    if (window.document.getElementsByName('to')[y].value==imgname && window.document.getElementsByName('toq')[y].value==seq) {
                        date1 = window.document.getElementsByName('tod')[y].value;
                    }
                }//end of for
            }
        }
    } else {
        date1 = '';
    }

    if (spnplace == 'spnfromi'){
        spnplace = 'spnf' + document.getElementById('fromi').value;
    }
    if (document.all("date"+spnplace)!=null){//決裁日期
        document.all("date"+spnplace).innerHTML  = "<font color=red size=1>"+date1+"</font>";
    }
    //(結束) 顯示決裁日期 

    //(開始) 顯示代理章 
    var agent_st='';
    var agtstr='';
	var agstr='';
    if ( seq == '' ) {
        //決裁
        if (window.document.getElementsByName('tod').length>1)    {
            for (y=1;y<window.document.getElementsByName('tod').length;y++)        {
                if (window.document.getElementsByName('to')[y].value==imgname && ( window.document.getElementsByName('tos')[y].value==1  || window.document.getElementsByName('tos')[y].value==2))     {
                    var tmpstr=window.document.getElementsByName('ton')[y].value;
                    if (tmpstr.slice(-4)=='(代理)') {
                        agent_st='Y';
                    }	 
                }
            }//END OF FOR
        }                     
    }
    if (agntname != '' || agent_st == 'Y') {
        agtstr = "<img src='../SIGN/AGENT.bmp'>";
    }
    //(結束) 顯示代理章		
    //不通過時要處裡可能殘留的前一個"日期"及"代理章"資料	
	if (COMPANYID !="B"){ 				
		if (parseFloat(mlevel) > 5){
			document.getElementById(spnplace).innerHTML = "<font color=red size=2><img src='../SIGN/" + imgname + ".bmp'>" + agtstr + "</font><INPUT TYPE=HIDDEN id=hid" + spnplace + " name=hid" + spnplace + ">";
		}
		else{//level=3 name display
			document.getElementById(spnplace).innerHTML = "<font color=red size=2>" + unescape(username) + "通過" + agtstr + "</font><INPUT TYPE=HIDDEN id=hid" + spnplace + " name=hid" + spnplace + ">";
		}
	}
	else {	
		//最新的寫法 20200219
		if (agntname != '' || agent_st == 'Y') {
			agstr = "<img src='../SIGN/AGENT.bmp'>";//代理章, 後面的 IF Statement 要配合修改使用 agstr才能顯示
		 }
		
		if (parseFloat(mlevel) >  5  )  { //預先載入
				document.getElementById(spnplace).innerHTML = "<font color=red size=2><img src='../SIGN/" + imgname + ".bmp'>" + agstr + "</font><INPUT TYPE=HIDDEN id=hid" + spnplace + " name=hid" + spnplace + ">";
			}
			else
			{//level=5以下用姓名表示 20200219
				if( imgname.length==3||imgname.length==5) 
				{ 
					document.getElementById(spnplace).innerHTML = "<font color=red size=2>" + unescape(username) + "通過" + agstr + "</font><INPUT TYPE=HIDDEN id=hid" + spnplace + " name=hid" + spnplace + ">";
				}
				
				else
				{
					var img = new Image();// 
					img.src = "../SIGN/" + imgname + ".bmp";
					window.document.getElementById(spnplace).innerHTML="<font color=red size=2><img src='../SIGN/" + imgname + ".bmp'>" + agstr + "</font><INPUT TYPE=HIDDEN id=hid" + spnplace + " name=hid" + spnplace + ">";   
				}
			
			}
	}	
	
		
		
}

//已存信件載入印章或評議
function old_impress_restore(st,imgname,username,mlevel,spnplace,imgplace,agntname,seq) {//20180607
    /*
	if (st == '3'){
		impress_onclick(imgname,username,mlevel,spnplace,imgplace);
		}
	else{
		document.all(spnplace).innerHTML = "<font color=red size=2><TEXTAREA rows=4 cols=16 id=are" + spnplace + " name=are" + spnplace + " readonly>" + imgname + "</TEXTAREA></font>";
		document.all('are' + spnplace).value = document.all(imgname).value
		}
	*/
    //20180607
    if (st == "3"){
        impress_onclick(imgname,username,mlevel,spnplace,imgplace,agntname,seq);
    }
 
    else{
        document.all(spnplace).innerHTML = "<font color=red size=2><TEXTAREA rows=3 cols=16 id=are" + spnplace + " name=are" + spnplace + " readonly>" + imgname + "</TEXTAREA></font>";
        document.all('are' + spnplace).value = document.all(imgname).value	
        if (document.all("date"+spnplace)!=null){//決裁日期
            document.all("date"+spnplace).innerHTML  = "<font color=red size=1></font>";
        }		
    }
}
//20040823
function selindataAll2() {
	for (i=0; i <  document.frmbdy.selindata1.length; i++){
		if ( i < 500){
			document.frmbdy.selindata1.options[i].selected = true;
			}
		else{
			document.frmbdy.selindata1.options[i].selected = false;
			var aElement = parent.frames['mail'].document.createElement('option');
			aElement.text = document.frmbdy.selindata1.options[i].text;
			parent.frames['mail'].frmbdy['selindata2'].options.add(aElement);			
			}
		}
		
	for (i=0; i <  document.frmbdy.selindata2.length; i++){
		document.frmbdy.selindata2.options[i].selected = true;
		}

	for (i=0; i <  document.frmbdy.selF70cfm1.length; i++){
		document.frmbdy.selF70cfm1.options[i].selected = true;
		}
}

//儲存
function btnsave_onclick(rc) {
	if(document.frmbdy.APPBUG.value=='' || document.frmbdy.APPBUG.value.length !=3){
		alert('預算單位[' + document.frmbdy.APPBUG.value + ']錯誤!畫面資料異常,請關閉再開啟.');
		return false;	
		}	

	if (rc == 'True') {
		tmpstr = '已經儲存過,是否再存一次?';
		}
	else {
		tmpstr = '是否儲存?';
		}
	if (window.confirm(tmpstr)){
		document.all.item("spanAcc1").style.display = '';
		document.all.item("spanAcc2").style.display = '';
		document.all.item("spanAcc3").style.display = '';
		document.all.item("spanAcc").style.display = '';
	
		if (document.frmbdy.selindata1.length > 1){
			document.all.item("spanTax").style.display = '';
			}
		else if (document.frmbdy.selindata1.length = 1){
			s = document.frmbdy.selindata1.options[0].text
			//window.prompt("--","test s=" + escape(s));
			s= s.substring(0,1)
			if ((s >= '0' && s <= '9') || (s >= 'A' && s <= 'Z')){ //20241224
			    document.all.item("spanTax").style.display = '';
				}
			}

		if (document.frmbdy['selF70cfm1'].length > 1){
			document.all.item("spanF70").style.display = '';
			}
		else if (document.frmbdy['selF70cfm1'].length = 1){
			s = document.frmbdy['selF70cfm1'].options[0].text
			s= s.substring(0,1)
			//alert("test s=" + s.length);
			if ((s >= '0' && s <= '9') || (s >= 'A' && s <= 'Z')){
			    document.all.item("spanF70").style.display = '';
			}
			else{ //20241224
			    document.frmbdy['selF70cfm1'].options.remove(0);
			}
		}

		oSum_onclick();
		document.frmbdy.hidsubmit.value = "save";
		//進項稅額
		document.all('errmsg1').innerText='訊息:儲存中,請稍後..';
		selindataAll2();
		document.frmbdy.submit();
		}
	else{
		//document.all.item("spanTax").style.display = 'none';	
		}		
}

//送出
function btnsend_onclick(DOCSTATUS) {
	if (document.frmbdy['STFLSTATUS'].value != "4"){
		if (checkhead2() == false){
			frmbdy.btnsend.disabled = true;
			return;
			}
		}
	if(document.frmbdy.APPBUG.value=='' || document.frmbdy.APPBUG.value.length !=3){
		alert('預算單位[' + document.frmbdy.APPBUG.value + ']錯誤!畫面資料異常,請關閉再開啟.');
		return false;	
		}	
	frmbdy.btnsend.disabled = true;
	document.all.item("spanAcc1").style.display = '';
	document.all.item("spanAcc2").style.display = '';
	document.all.item("spanAcc3").style.display = '';
	document.all.item("spanAcc").style.display = '';
	if (document.frmbdy.selindata1.length > 1){
		document.all.item("spanTax").style.display = '';
		}
	else if (document.frmbdy.selindata1.length = 1){
		s = document.frmbdy.selindata1.options[0].text
		s= s.substring(0,1)
		if ((s >= '0' && s <= '9') || (s >= 'A' && s <= 'Z')){ //20241224
			document.all.item("spanTax").style.display = '';
			}
	}
    //20241224
	if (document.frmbdy['selF70cfm1'].length > 1){
	    document.all.item("spanF70").style.display = '';
	}
	else if (document.frmbdy['selF70cfm1'].length = 1){
	    s = document.frmbdy['selF70cfm1'].options[0].text
	    s= s.substring(0,1)
	    if ((s >= '0' && s <= '9') || (s >= 'A' && s <= 'Z')){
	        document.all.item("spanF70").style.display = '';
	    }
	    else{ //20241224
	        document.frmbdy['selF70cfm1'].options.remove(0);
	    }
	}
	if ((DOCSTATUS != 'B')){
		oSum_onclick();
		if (checkhead() == false){
			frmbdy.btnsend.disabled = false;
			return;
			}
		}	
	
	tmpstr = '是否送出?';
	//不詢問,直接送出	
	//2000/10/11
	if (chkspnplace.length == 5){
		if (checkare() == false){
			frmbdy.btnsend.disabled = false;
			return;
			}
		}
		
	document.all('errmsg').innerText='';	
	document.all('runmsg').innerText='訊息:送出處理中,請稍候.';
	document.frmbdy.hidsubmit.value = "send";
	selindataAll2();
	document.frmbdy.submit();
}

//2000/10/11檢查評語
function old_checkare() {
	inttmp = document.frmbdy['are'+chkspnplace].value.length ;
	if (inttmp > 20){
		window.alert('對不起!!您的評語共' + inttmp + '字,不能超過20字!');
		return false;		
		}
	return true;
}

//載入視窗事件
function window_onload(strmd,strSt,strcf) {
	try{
		parent.opener.parent.frames['main'].document.all('inopenwin').value -= -1;
		}
	catch(e){}
	
	parent.window.moveTo(0,0);
	var wheight1=screen.availHeight;
	var wwidth1=screen.availWidth;
	parent.window.resizeTo(wwidth1,wheight1);
    //addrow_onload();
	document.all("runmsg").innerText="";
	show();

	document.frmbdy.scrollIntoView();
	
	if (((strmd == '99') && strcf != 'Y') || (strSt != 'B' && strSt != 'C')){
		frmbdy.btnsave.disabled = false;
		}	
		
	
	
}
//釋放視窗事件
function window_onunload_other(){
    //new
}

var cnt_unload = 0;
function old_window_onunload() {
	//alert("");
	cnt_unload += 1;
	if (cnt_unload>1) {
		parent.opener.parent.frames['right'].location.reload();
		return;}
	try{
		parent.opener.parent.frames['main'].document.all('inopenwin').value -=  1;
		parent.opener.parent.frames['right'].location.reload();
		}
	catch(e){}
}

//關閉
function old_btnclose_onclick() {
	try{
		parent.opener.parent.frames['right'].location.reload();
		}
	catch(e){}
	//alert("TEST");
	parent.window.close(); 
	window.setTimeout("parent.opener.parent.frames['main'].document.all('inopenwin').value -= 1;parent.window.location.href='about:blank';",500);	
}

//特殊字元檢查
function Chartest_onchange(A1){
	var re;
	var Chkstring=A1.value;
	if (Chkstring!=''){
		re = /[\x22\x27\x5c\x26\x23\x3c\x3d\x3e\x3f\x7b\x7d]/g;
		Chkstring=Chkstring.replace(re, "~"); 

		re = /(--)/g;
		Chkstring=Chkstring.replace(re, "~"); 
		re = "/*";
		Chkstring=Chkstring.replace(re, "~"); 
		re = "*/";
		Chkstring=Chkstring.replace(re, "~"); 
		
		A1.value=Chkstring
		}		
}

function POBJNO_onkeyup() {
	var objchk=document.frmbdy.POBJNO.value;
	if (objchk.length==6){
		document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.focus();
		}
	else{
		return;
		}
}

function POBJNO_onblur() {
	if (document.frmbdy.onbluecnt.value=='Y'){
		return;
		}
	document.frmbdy.onbluecnt.value='Y';	
	if (document.frmbdy.POBJNO.value==''){
		document.frmbdy.onbluecnt.value='';
		return;
		}
	var chk=document.frmbdy.POBJNO.value;
	if 	(chk.substring(0,1)==' '){
		document.frmbdy.POBJNO.value='';
		alert('會計科目不可空白');
		document.frmbdy.POBJNO.focus();
		document.frmbdy.onbluecnt.value='';
		return;
		}	
			
	var actno=document.frmbdy.POBJNO.value;
	document.frmbdy.onbluecnt.value='Y';
	parent.frames['FIND'].location.href = 'PEPH6102.asp?ACTION=actnoget&ACTNO1='+actno+'&ACTNO2='+actno + '&BUGAREA=' + parent.frames['mail'].frmbdy.SELTOCOMP.value +'&T='+'20260126113634';

}

}

function PITEMNO_onblur() {
	if (document.frmbdy.onbluecnt.value=='Y'){
		document.frmbdy.POBJNO.focus();
		return;
		}

		alert('請先輸入會計科目');
		document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value='';
		document.frmbdy.HPITEMNO.value='';
		document.frmbdy.POBJNO.focus();
		document.frmbdy.onbluecnt.value='';
		return;
		}	
	var actno=document.frmbdy.POBJNO.value;
	var actitno=document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value;
	document.frmbdy.ITMGET.disabled=true;
	document.frmbdy.BUGGET.disabled=true;

		actitno='';
		}

}

function PBUGNO_onblur() {
	if (document.frmbdy.onbluecnt.value=='Y'){
		document.frmbdy.PMEMONO.focus();
		return;
		}
	document.frmbdy.onbluecnt.value='Y';	
	if (document.frmbdy.PBUGNO.value==''){
		document.frmbdy.HPBUGNO.value='';
		document.frmbdy.onbluecnt.value='';
		return;
		}
	var chk=document.frmbdy.PBUGNO.value;
	if 	(chk.substring(0,1)==' '){
		document.frmbdy.PBUGNO.value='';
		document.frmbdy.HPBUGNO.value='';
		alert('預算單位不可空白');
		document.frmbdy.PBUGNO.focus();
		document.frmbdy.onbluecnt.value='';
		return;
		}	
		
	var bugvno=document.frmbdy.PBUGNO.value;
	bugvno=bugvno.toUpperCase();
	document.frmbdy.PBUGNO.value=bugvno;
	parent.frames['FIND'].location.href = 'PEPH6102.asp?ACTION=bugget&BUGVNO=' + bugvno + '&bugarea=' + document.frmbdy.SELTOCOMP.value +'&T='+'20260126113634';
}

function PCREAD_onblur() {
	var chk=document.frmbdy.PCREAD.value;
	if 	(chk.substring(0,1)==''){
		return;
		}	
	if 	(chk.substring(0,1)==' '){
		document.frmbdy.PCREAD.value='';
		return;
		}	
	if (isNaN(parseInt(document.frmbdy.PCREAD.value))){
		alert('金額請輸入數字');
		document.frmbdy.PCREAD.value='';
		document.frmbdy.PCREAD.focus();
		return;
		}	
	if (parseInt(document.frmbdy.PCREAD.value,10)<0){
		alert('金額不可為負數');
		document.frmbdy.PCREAD.value='';
		document.frmbdy.PCREAD.focus();
		return;
		}
	if (trncard == '002') {
		document.frmbdy.PCREAD.value=Math.round(parseFloat(document.frmbdy.PCREAD.value)*100)/100;
		}
	else{
		document.frmbdy.PCREAD.value=Math.abs(parseInt(document.frmbdy.PCREAD.value,10));
		}
}

function PCOMPNO_onblur(trncard) {
	var chk=document.frmbdy.PCOMPNO.value;
	if 	(chk.substring(0,1)==''){
		document.frmbdy.HPCOMPNO.value='';
		return;
		}	
	if 	(chk.substring(0,1)==' '){
		document.frmbdy.PCOMPNO.value='';
		document.frmbdy.HPCOMPNO.value='';
		return;
		}	
	if 	(chk.length != 8){
		document.frmbdy.PCOMPNO.value='';
		document.frmbdy.HPCOMPNO.value='';
		return;
		}	
	var compno=document.frmbdy.PCOMPNO.value;
	compno=compno.toUpperCase();
	document.frmbdy.PCOMPNO.value=compno;
	parent.frames['FIND'].location.href = 'PEPH6102.asp?ACTION=compnoget&PCOMPNO=' + compno + '&trncard=' + trncard  + '&BUGAREA=' + parent.frames['mail'].frmbdy.SELTOCOMP.value +'&T='+'20260126113634';
}

//202308 電子發票
function PINVONO_onkeyup() {
	var objchk=document.frmbdy.PINVONO.value;
	if (objchk.length==10){
		document.frmbdy.PPAYDOC.focus();
		}
	else{
		return;
		}
}

function PINVONO_onblur() {
	var chk=document.frmbdy.PINVONO.value;
	if 	(chk.substring(0,1)==''){
		document.frmbdy.HPINVONO.value='';
		return;
		}	
	if (chk.length<10){
		document.frmbdy.PINVONO.value='';
		document.frmbdy.HPINVONO.value='';
		alert('發票型態不對');
		return;
	}
	if 	(chk.substring(0,1)==' '){
		document.frmbdy.PINVONO.value='';
		document.frmbdy.HPINVONO.value='';
		return;
		}
	var chktype='1';		
	if 	(isNaN(parseInt(chk.substring(0,1)))){
		if 	(isNaN(parseInt(chk.substring(1,2)))){
			if (isNaN(parseInt(chk.substring(2,10)))){
				alert(parseInt(chk.substring(2,10)));
				document.frmbdy.PINVONO.value='';
				document.frmbdy.HPINVONO.value='';
				alert('發票型態不對');
				return;
				}
			if (parseInt(chk.substring(2,10))<1000000){
				var chknum=0;
				for (i=2;i<10;i++){
					if(isNaN(parseInt(chk.substring(i,i+1)))){
						chknum=1;
						}
					}	
				if(chknum==1){
					document.frmbdy.PINVONO.value='';
					document.frmbdy.HPINVONO.value='';
					alert('發票型態不對');
					return;
					}	
				}
			}
		else{
			document.frmbdy.PINVONO.value='';
			document.frmbdy.HPINVONO.value='';
			alert('發票型態不對');
			return;
			}	
		}	
	else{
		document.frmbdy.PINVONO.value='';
		document.frmbdy.HPINVONO.value='';
		alert('發票型態不對');
		return;
		}	
	document.frmbdy.PINVONO.value=chk.toUpperCase();
	document.frmbdy.HPINVONO.value=chk.toUpperCase();
	return;
}

function PPAYDOC_onblur() {
	Chartest_onchange(document.frmbdy.PPAYDOC);
	checklength(event.srcElement.id);
	try{document.frmbdy.ADD1.focus();}
		catch(e){return;}
	return;
}

function TAXMONEY_onfocus() {
	var ss,scount,nvalue;
	//ss=document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY.value.split(',');
	if (event.srcElement.id !='TAXMONEY' && event.srcElement.id !='TAXMONEY2')
		return;
	ss=event.srcElement.value.split(',');
	scount=ss.length;
	nvalue='';
	for (i=0;i<scount;i++){
		nvalue=nvalue+ss[i];
		}
	//document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY.value=nvalue;
	event.srcElement.value=nvalue;  
}

//	TAXMONEY_onfocus(); 
//}

function TAXMONEY_onblur() {
	var chk=document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY.value;
	var chk4=document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY2.value;
	
	if 	(chk.substring(0,1)=='0' && chk.substring(0,2) !='0.'){
		document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY.value='0';
		}	
	else if (chk.substring(0,1)=='' || chk.substring(0,1)==' '){
		document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY.value='0';
		}	
	else if (isNaN(parseInt(document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY.value))){
		alert('金額請輸入數字');
		document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY.value='0';
		document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY.focus();
		}	
	else if (parseInt(document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY.value,10)<0){
		alert('金額不可為負數');
		document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY.value='0';
		document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY.focus();
		}	
	else if (isNaN(parseInt(document.frmbdy.TotalC.value))){
		alert('請先輸入合計金額');
		document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY.value='0';
		document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY.focus();
		}

	if 	(chk4.substring(0,1)=='0' && chk4.substring(0,2) !='0.'){
		document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY2.value='0';
		}	
	else if (chk4.substring(0,1)=='' || chk4.substring(0,1)==' '){
		document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY2.value='0';
		}	
	else if (isNaN(parseInt(document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY2.value))){
		alert('金額請輸入數字');
		document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY2.value='0';
		document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY2.focus();
		}	
	else if (parseInt(document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY2.value,10)<0){
		alert('金額不可為負數');
		document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY2.value='0';
		document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY2.focus();
		}	
	else if (isNaN(parseInt(document.frmbdy.TotalC.value))){
		alert('請先輸入合計金額');
		document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY2.value='0';
		document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY2.focus();
		}
	
	document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY.value = DeAddCommaH(document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY.value);
	document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY2.value = DeAddCommaH(document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY2.value);		
	if (parseInt(document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY.value,10) + parseInt(document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY2.value,10)>parseInt(document.frmbdy.TotalC.value,10)){	
		alert('扣繳不可大於合計金額');
		if (parseInt(document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY.value,10) >= parseInt(document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY2.value,10)){
			document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY.value='0';
			document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY.focus();
			}
		else {
			document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY2.value='0';
			document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY2.focus();
			}
		}
		
	if (trncard == '002') {
		chk = Math.round(parseFloat(document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY.value)*100)/100;
		chk4 = Math.round(parseFloat(document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY2.value)*100)/100;
		}
	else{
		chk = Math.abs(parseInt(document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY.value,10));
		chk4 = Math.abs(parseInt(document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY2.value,10));
		}

	var chk2=document.frmbdy.TotalC.value;
	
	var chk3=0;
	if (trncard == '001') {
		if (document.frmbdy.hdAMT.value != ''){
			chk3 = parseInt(DeAddCommaH(document.frmbdy.hdAMT.value),10);
			}
		}

	document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY.value = chk;
	document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY2.value = chk4;
	document.frmbdy.RGMONEY.value = chk2-chk-chk4-chk3;
	if (trncard == '002') {
		document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY.value = AddCommaH(document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY.value);
		document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY2.value = AddCommaH(document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY2.value);
		document.frmbdy.RGMONEY.value  = AddCommaH(document.frmbdy.RGMONEY.value);
		}
	else{		
		document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY.value = AddComma(document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY.value);
		document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY2.value = AddComma(document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY2.value);
		document.frmbdy.RGMONEY.value  = AddComma(document.frmbdy.RGMONEY.value);
		}
		

}

//輸入各欄檢查函式結束+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++

//資料新增一筆
function ADD1_onclick() {
	if (document.frmbdy.onbluecnt.value=='Y'){
		return;
		}
	if(document.frmbdy.oRowcnt.value=='12' && document.frmbdy.oSpacnt.value=='0'){
		alert('資料筆數不可超過12筆');
		return;
		}
	//if(document.frmbdy.POBJNO.value=='4001-1'){ //改用設定
	//	alert('請求付款傳票不可使用此科目!');
	//	return;
	//	}
	if(document.frmbdy.POBJNO.value=='' || document.frmbdy.POBJNO.value.substring(0,1)==' '){
		alert('科目不可空白');
		return;
		}
	if(document.frmbdy.PBUGNO.value=='' || document.frmbdy.PBUGNO.value.substring(0,1)==' '){
		alert('單位不可空白');
		return;
		}	
	if(document.frmbdy.PCREAD.value=='' || document.frmbdy.PCREAD.value=='0'){
		alert('金額不可空白');
		return;
		}		
	if(document.frmbdy.PCREAD.value.length > 11){
		alert('金額位數超過');
		return;
		}		
	if (trncard == '004'){		
		if ( document.frmbdy.PCOMPNO.value=='' || document.frmbdy.PCOMPNO.value==' '){
			alert('廠商統一編號不可空白');
			return;
			}	
		}
	if (document.frmbdy.POBJNAME.value==''){
			alert('科目名稱空白，請確認科目');
			return;
		}		
	if(document.frmbdy.POBJNO.value!=document.frmbdy.HPOBJNO.value){
		return;
		}
	if(document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value!=document.frmbdy.HPITEMNO.value){
		return;
		}
	if(document.frmbdy.PMEMONO.value!=document.frmbdy.HPMEMONO.value){
		return;
		}		
	if(document.frmbdy.PBUGNO.value!=document.frmbdy.HPBUGNO.value){
		return;
		}			
	if (document.frmbdy.PCOMPNO.value!=document.frmbdy.HPCOMPNO.value){			
			return;
			}		
	document.frmbdy.AccConfirm.value='';	
	objin=document.frmbdy.POBJNO.value;
	itemin=document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value;
	bugin=document.frmbdy.PBUGNO.value;
	menoin=document.frmbdy.PMEMONO.value;
	paydocin=document.frmbdy.PPAYDOC.value;
	objnamein=document.frmbdy.POBJNAME.value;
	invoin=document.frmbdy.PINVONO.value;
	compno=document.frmbdy.PCOMPNO.value;
	creadin=document.frmbdy.PCREAD.value;
	ELECINVO=document.frmbdy.ELECINVO.value; //電子發票廠商註記
	PAYTYPE= document.frmbdy.PAYTYPE.value;
	if (Math.abs(document.frmbdy.oSpacnt.value) > 0 ){
		//Update
		rowcnt = Math.abs(document.frmbdy.oRowcnt.value) - Math.abs(document.frmbdy.oSpacnt.value);
		addcnt = parseInt(document.form2.selRow.options[rowcnt].value) ;
		oAddRow_onclick('U', rowcnt, addcnt,objin,itemin,bugin,menoin,paydocin,objnamein,invoin,compno,creadin);
		}
	else{
		//Insert 	
		rowcnt = Math.abs(document.frmbdy.oRowcnt.value);
		addcnt = Math.abs(document.frmbdy.oAddcnt.value)
		oAddRow_onclick('A',rowcnt, addcnt,objin,itemin,bugin,menoin,paydocin,objnamein,invoin,compno,creadin);
		}
	document.frmbdy.POBJNO.focus();
	SELinterComp_cal('add','');
	//進項稅額
	if(document.frmbdy.POBJNO.value=='2302-3' && (document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='03' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='05')){
		document.all.item("spanTax").style.display = '';
		document.all.item("spanAcc1").style.display = 'none';
		document.all.item("spanAcc2").style.display = 'none';
		document.all.item("spanAcc3").style.display = 'none';
		document.all.item("spanAcc").style.display = 'none';
		document.all("spninmsg").innerText = "";
		document.frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.value = document.frmbdy.PCOMPNO.value;
		document.frmbdy.UNITIVEND.value = document.frmbdy.PINVONO.value;		
		document.frmbdy.CHKIND.focus();
		if (document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='05'){
			document.frmbdy.CHKIND.value = '5';
			}
		}
	/*if(((document.frmbdy.POBJNO.value=='5318-0' || document.frmbdy.POBJNO.value=='4318-0') && (document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='01' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='02' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='03' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='04' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='06' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='10' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='99' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='A1' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='A2' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='A3' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='A4' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='A6')) || ((document.frmbdy.POBJNO.value == '5409-1' || document.frmbdy.POBJNO.value == '4409-1') && (document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='01' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='02' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='05' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='14' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='A1' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='A3' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='A8' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='26' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='B6')  ) || ((document.frmbdy.POBJNO.value == '5319-0' || document.frmbdy.POBJNO.value == '4319-0') && (document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='01' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='02' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='A1' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='A2'))){
		document.all.item("spanF70").style.display = '';
		document.all.item("spanAcc1").style.display = 'none';
		document.all.item("spanAcc2").style.display = 'none';
		document.all.item("spanAcc3").style.display = 'none';
		document.all.item("spanAcc").style.display = 'none';
		document.all("spninmsg").innerText = "";
		document.frmbdy.CFMNO.focus();
		}*/

	//202310 電子發票擴大 如ELECINVO有值則為電子發票廠商分類0且不可手打輸入,反之則不顯示電子發票選用按鈕需手打輸入
	//202311 台幣電匯員工PAYTYPE=1 則不控制電子發票手打或選用
	if(ELECINVO != '' && PAYTYPE != 1){ 
		document.frmbdy.CHKIND.value = '0';
		document.frmbdy.YYYYMM.disabled = true;
		document.frmbdy.UNITIVEND.disabled = true;
		document.frmbdy.AMT.disabled = true;
		document.frmbdy.TAXAMT.disabled = true;
		document.frmbdy.CHCNT.disabled = true;
		// document.frmbdy.btneinvoice.style.visibility  = 'visible';
		document.frmbdy.btneinvoice.removeAttribute("disabled");
	}else{
		document.frmbdy.CHKIND.value = '';
		document.frmbdy.YYYYMM.disabled = false;
		document.frmbdy.UNITIVEND.disabled = false;
		document.frmbdy.AMT.disabled = false;
		document.frmbdy.TAXAMT.disabled = false;
		document.frmbdy.CHCNT.disabled = false;
		// document.frmbdy.btneinvoice.style.visibility  = 'hidden';
		document.frmbdy.btneinvoice.setAttribute("disabled", "disabled");
	}

	document.frmbdy.Corind.value='';	
	document.frmbdy.POBJNO.value='';
	document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value='';
	document.frmbdy.PBUGNO.value='';
	document.frmbdy.PMEMONO.value='';
	document.frmbdy.PPAYDOC.value='';
	document.frmbdy.POBJNAME.value='';
	document.frmbdy.PINVONO.value='';
	document.frmbdy.PCOMPNO.value='';
	//隱藏欄位
	document.frmbdy.HPOBJNO.value='';
	document.frmbdy.HPITEMNO.value='';
	document.frmbdy.HPBUGNO.value='';
	document.frmbdy.HPMEMONO.value='';
	document.frmbdy.HPINVONO.value='';
	document.frmbdy.HPCOMPNO.value='';
	//***********************
	document.frmbdy.PCREAD.value='';
	document.frmbdy.ADD1.disabled=false;
	document.frmbdy.UPD1.disabled=true;
	document.frmbdy.DEL1.disabled=true;
	document.frmbdy.ITMGET.disabled=false;
	document.frmbdy.BUGGET.disabled=false;
}
//已輸入資料更正 將資料取出至更正位置
function COR1_onclick(A1) {
	if(document.all['OBJNO' +A1].value!='' || document.all['OBJNAME' +A1].value!=''){
		document.frmbdy.POBJNO.value=document.all['OBJNO' +A1].value;
		document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=document.all['ITEMNO' +A1].value;
		document.frmbdy.PBUGNO.value=document.all['BUGNO' +A1].value;
		document.frmbdy.PMEMONO.value=document.all['MEMONO' +A1].value;
		document.frmbdy.HPOBJNO.value=document.all['OBJNO' +A1].value;
		document.frmbdy.HPITEMNO.value=document.all['ITEMNO' +A1].value;
		document.frmbdy.HPBUGNO.value=document.all['BUGNO' +A1].value;
		document.frmbdy.HPMEMONO.value=document.all['MEMONO' +A1].value;
		document.frmbdy.PPAYDOC.value=document.all['PAYDOCU' +A1].value+document.all['PAYDOCL' +A1].value;
	
			
		if (trncard == '002') {
			document.frmbdy.PPAYDOC.value=document.all['PAYDOCU' +A1].value;
			}
	
		
		document.frmbdy.POBJNAME.value=document.all['OBJNAME' +A1].value;
		document.frmbdy.PINVONO.value=document.all['INVONO' +A1].value;
		document.frmbdy.PCOMPNO.value=document.all['COMPNO' +A1].value;
		document.frmbdy.HPINVONO.value=document.all['INVONO' +A1].value;
		document.frmbdy.HPCOMPNO.value=document.all['COMPNO' +A1].value;
		document.frmbdy.PCREAD.value=document.all['CREAD' +A1].value;
		
	
		document.frmbdy.ADD1.disabled=true;	
		
		document.frmbdy.UPD1.disabled=false;
		document.frmbdy.Corind.value=A1;	
		document.frmbdy.POBJNO.focus();		
		}

	var compno=document.frmbdy.PCOMPNO.value; //加入判斷電子發票廠商
	parent.frames['FIND'].location.href = 'PEPH6102.asp?ACTION=chkcompany&PCOMPNO=' + compno +'&T='+ '20260126113634';
}

function UPD1_onclick() {

		alert('科目不可空白');
		return;
		}
	if(document.frmbdy.PBUGNO.value=='' || document.frmbdy.PBUGNO.value.substring(0,1)==' '){
		alert('單位不可空白');
		return;
		}	
	if(document.frmbdy.PCREAD.value=='' || document.frmbdy.PCREAD.value=='0'){
		alert('金額不可空白');
		return;
		}				
	if(document.frmbdy.PCREAD.value.length > 11){
		alert('金額位數超過');
		return;
		}		
	if (trncard == '004'){	
		if ( document.frmbdy.PCOMPNO.value=='' || document.frmbdy.PCOMPNO.value==' '){
			alert('廠商統一編號不可空白');
			return;
			}
		}		
	if (document.frmbdy.POBJNAME.value==''){
			alert('科目名稱空白，請確認科目');
			return;
		}
	if(document.frmbdy.POBJNO.value!=document.frmbdy.HPOBJNO.value){
		return;
		}
	if(document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value!=document.frmbdy.HPITEMNO.value){
		return;
		}
	if(document.frmbdy.PMEMONO.value!=document.frmbdy.HPMEMONO.value){
		return;
		}		
	if(document.frmbdy.PBUGNO.value!=document.frmbdy.HPBUGNO.value){
		return;
		}			
	if (document.frmbdy.PCOMPNO.value!=document.frmbdy.HPCOMPNO.value){			
			return;
			}		
	var A1=document.frmbdy.Corind.value;

	ELECINVO=document.frmbdy.ELECINVO.value; //電子發票廠商註記
	//202310 電子發票擴大 如ELECINVO有值則為電子發票廠商分類0且不可手打輸入,反之則不顯示電子發票選用按鈕需手打輸入
	if(ELECINVO!=''){

	}else{

		document.frmbdy.YYYYMM.disabled = false;
		document.frmbdy.UNITIVEND.disabled = false;
		document.frmbdy.AMT.disabled = false;
		document.frmbdy.TAXAMT.disabled = false;
		document.frmbdy.CHCNT.disabled = false;
		// document.frmbdy.btneinvoice.style.visibility  = 'hidden';
		document.frmbdy.btneinvoice.setAttribute("disabled", "disabled");
	}

	if (A1!=''){
		SELinterComp_cal('upd',A1);
		document.all['OBJNO' +A1].value=document.frmbdy.POBJNO.value;
		document.all['ITEMNO' +A1].value=document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value;
		document.all['BUGNO' +A1].value=document.frmbdy.PBUGNO.value;
		document.all['MEMONO' +A1].value=document.frmbdy.PMEMONO.value;
		document.all['PAYDOCU' +A1].value = BSubstr(document.frmbdy.PPAYDOC.value,0,20)
		 
		if (trncard != '002') {
			document.all['PAYDOCL' +A1].value = BSubstr(document.frmbdy.PPAYDOC.value,20,40);		
			}
		else{
	
			}

		//進項稅額
		if(document.frmbdy.POBJNO.value=='2302-3' && (document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='03' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='05')){
			document.all.item("spanTax").style.display = '';
			document.all.item("spanAcc1").style.display = 'none';
			document.all.item("spanAcc2").style.display = 'none';
			document.all.item("spanAcc3").style.display = 'none';
			document.all.item("spanAcc").style.display = 'none';
			document.all("spninmsg").innerText = "";
			document.frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.value = document.frmbdy.PCOMPNO.value;
			document.frmbdy.UNITIVEND.value = document.frmbdy.PINVONO.value;

				document.frmbdy.CHKIND.value = '5';
				}
			}

		/*if(((document.frmbdy.POBJNO.value=='5318-0' || document.frmbdy.POBJNO.value=='4318-0') && (document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='01' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='02' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='03' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='04' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='06' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='10' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='99' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='A1' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='A2' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='A3' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='A4' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='A6')) || ((document.frmbdy.POBJNO.value == '5409-1' || document.frmbdy.POBJNO.value == '4409-1') && (document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='01' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='02' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='05' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='14' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='A1' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='A3' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='A8' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='26' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='B6')  ) || ((document.frmbdy.POBJNO.value == '5319-0' || document.frmbdy.POBJNO.value == '4319-0') && (document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='01' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='02' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='A1' || document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value=='A2'))){
			document.all.item("spanF70").style.display = '';
			document.all.item("spanAcc1").style.display = 'none';
			document.all.item("spanAcc2").style.display = 'none';
			document.all.item("spanAcc3").style.display = 'none';

			document.frmbdy.CFMNO.focus();
			}*/

		document.all['OBJNAME' +A1].value=document.frmbdy.POBJNAME.value;

		document.all['COMPNO' +A1].value=document.frmbdy.PCOMPNO.value;
		document.all['CREAD' +A1].value=document.frmbdy.PCREAD.value;
		document.all['Desc' +A1].value='';
		
		if (trncard == '002'){
			document.all['CREADV' + A1].value = AddCommaH(document.all['CREAD' +A1].value);
			}
		else{
			document.all['CREADV' + A1].value = AddComma(document.all['CREAD' +A1].value);
			}
		document.frmbdy.Corind.value='';

		document.frmbdy.PBUGNO.value='';
		document.frmbdy.PMEMONO.value='';
		document.frmbdy.PPAYDOC.value='';
		document.frmbdy.POBJNAME.value='';
		document.frmbdy.PINVONO.value='';
		document.frmbdy.PCOMPNO.value='';
		document.frmbdy.HPOBJNO.value='';
		document.frmbdy.HPITEMNO.value='';
		document.frmbdy.HPBUGNO.value='';
		document.frmbdy.HPMEMONO.value='';
		document.frmbdy.HPINVONO.value='';
		document.frmbdy.HPCOMPNO.value='';
		document.frmbdy.PCREAD.value='';
	
		document.frmbdy.AccConfirm.value='';	
		oSum_onclick();				
		document.frmbdy.UPD1.disabled=true;
		document.frmbdy.DEL1.disabled=true;		
		}

}
//資料刪除
function DEL1_onclick() {
	if (document.frmbdy.onbluecnt.value=='Y'){
		return;
		}	

	var A1=document.frmbdy.Corind.value;
    if (A1!=''){
		SELinterComp_cal('del',A1);
		var rowcount=parseInt(document.frmbdy.oRowcnt.value);
		for (var icount1 = 1; icount1< rowcount+1; icount1++)
			{
			if (document.form2.selRow.options[icount1-1].value==A1)
				{
				dd=icount1;
				break;
				}
			}
		j = document.form2.selRow.options[dd-1].value;
		var temp = 'CREAD';
		temp = temp +A1;
		document.frmbdy.TotalC.value = (Math.abs(document.frmbdy.TotalC.value)*10 -  Math.abs(document.frmbdy[temp].value)*10)/10;

//增加,維護一列
function oAddRow_onclick(strcd,rowcnt,addcnt,objin,itemin,bugin,menoin,paydocin,objnamein,invoin,compno,creadin) {
	rowcnt = parseInt(rowcnt) + 1;
	addcnt = parseInt(addcnt) + 1;
	var addcnt1 = addcnt-1 ;
	if (strcd == 'A'){
		otbl.insertRow(rowcnt);
		document.frmbdy.oAddcnt.value = Math.abs(document.frmbdy.oAddcnt.value) + 1;
		document.frmbdy.oRowcnt.value = Math.abs(document.frmbdy.oRowcnt.value) + 1;
		var aElement = document.createElement('option');
		aElement.value = addcnt;
		aElement.text = addcnt;    
		document.form2.selRow.options.add(aElement);	
		}
	else if (strcd == 'U'){
		otbl.deleteRow(rowcnt);
		otbl.insertRow(rowcnt);
		document.frmbdy.oSpacnt.value = Math.abs(document.frmbdy.oSpacnt.value) - 1;
		}	
	for (i=0;i<6;i++){
	otbl.rows[rowcnt].insertCell();
	}
	
		var aclick='';	
		
	
	otbl.rows[rowcnt].cells[0].width=200;
	var a='<TABLE BORDER=0  cellPadding="0" cellSpacing="0" ' + aclick + '  WIDTH=100%><tr>';
	a=a + '<TD COLSPAN=2  align=center style="border:thin solid silver;border-top:none;border-left:none;border-right:none;">';
	a=a + '<INPUT type="text" id=OBJNAME' + addcnt1 + ' name=OBJNAME' + addcnt1 + ' size=22 value="' + objnamein + '" style="border:none;text-align: left;font-size:14px" readonly>';
	a=a + '</TD></TR><TR>';
	
	a=a + '<TD align=center style="width:140px;border:thin solid silver;border-top:none;border-bottom:none;border-left:none;">';
	a=a + '<INPUT type="text" id=OBJNO' + addcnt1 + ' name=OBJNO' + addcnt1 + '  value="' + objin + '" style="width:100%;border:none;text-align:center;font-size:16px" readonly>';

	a=a + '</TD><TD align=center style="width:60px;border:thin solid silver;border-top:none;border-bottom:none;border-left:none;border-right:none;">';
	a=a + '<INPUT type="text" id=ITEMNO' + addcnt1 + ' name=ITEMNO' + addcnt1 + '   value="' + itemin + '" style="width:100%;border:none;text-align:center;font-size:16px" readonly>';

	otbl.rows[rowcnt].cells[0].insertAdjacentHTML('beforeEnd',a);
	
	otbl.rows[rowcnt].cells[1].width=45;
	var b= '<TABLE BORDER=0 cellPadding="0" cellSpacing="0" ' + aclick + ' WIDTH=100%><TR>';
	b=b + '<TD align=center style="border:thin solid silver;border-top:none;border-left:none;border-right:none;">';
	b=b + '<INPUT type="text" id=MEMONO' + addcnt1 + ' name=MEMONO' + addcnt1 + ' value="' + menoin + '" style="width:100%;border:none;text-align: center;font-size:16px" readonly>';
	b=b + '</TD></TR><TR>';
	
	b=b + '<TD align=center style="border:thin solid silver;border-top:none;border-bottom:none;border-left:none;border-right:none;">';
	b=b + '<INPUT type="text" id=BUGNO' + addcnt1 + ' name=BUGNO' + addcnt1 + ' value="' + bugin + '" style="width:100%;border:none;text-align: center;font-size:16px" readonly>';
	b=b + '</TD></TR></TABLE>';
	otbl.rows[rowcnt].cells[1].insertAdjacentHTML('beforeEnd',b);
	
	otbl.rows[rowcnt].cells[2].width=120;
	var c='<INPUT type="text" id=CREADV' + addcnt1 + ' name=CREADV' + addcnt1 + ' value="" style="width:100%;border:none;text-align: right;font-size:16px" readonly>';
	c=c + '<INPUT type="HIDDEN" id=CREAD' + addcnt1 + ' name=CREAD' + addcnt1 + ' value="' + creadin + '" style="border:none;text-align: right;font-size:16px" readonly>';
	otbl.rows[rowcnt].cells[2].insertAdjacentHTML('beforeEnd',c);	

	if (trncard == '002' && document.all['CREAD' + addcnt1].value != ''){

		}
	else
		{

		}

	d=d + '<TD align=center style="border:thin solid silver;border-top:none;border-left:none;border-right:none;">';

	d=d + '</TD></TR></TABLE>';
	otbl.rows[rowcnt].cells[3].insertAdjacentHTML('beforeEnd',d);	
	
	otbl.rows[rowcnt].cells[4].width=170;
	var e='<TABLE BORDER=0 cellPadding="0" cellSpacing="0" ' + aclick + ' width=100%><TR>';
	e=e + '<TD style="">';
	e=e + '<INPUT type="text" id=PAYDOCU' + addcnt1 + ' name=PAYDOCU' + addcnt1 + ' size=20 value="' + BSubstr(paydocin,0,20) + '" style="border:none;text-align:left;font-size:14px" readonly>';

	e=e + '</TD></TR><TR>';

	e=e + '</TD></TR></TABLE>';
	otbl.rows[rowcnt].cells[4].insertAdjacentHTML('beforeEnd',e);	
	
	
	
	oSum_onclick();
	
}

//合計
function oSum_onclick() {	
	var zerochk=document.frmbdy.oSpacnt.value;
	if (zerochk==14){
		return;
		}
	var dd = document.frmbdy.oRowcnt.value;
	dd=dd-zerochk;
	if (dd > 0) {			
		var totalc=0;		
		for (icount = 0; icount < dd; icount++){
			var temp = 'CREAD';
			temp = temp + document.form2.selRow.options[icount].value;
			if ( Math.abs(document.frmbdy[temp].value ) > 0) {
				totalc = (totalc * 10 +  Math.abs(document.frmbdy[temp].value)*10)/10;
				}
			}
			
		if (trncard == '002'){
			totalc = Math.round(totalc*100)/100;
			document.frmbdy.TotalC.value=totalc;
			document.frmbdy.TotalC1.value = AddCommaH(document.frmbdy.TotalC.value);
			}
		else{
			document.frmbdy.TotalC.value=totalc;
			document.frmbdy.TotalC1.value = AddComma(document.frmbdy.TotalC.value);
			}
			
		//var ss,scount,chk;
		//ss=document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY.value.split(',');
		//scount=ss.length;
		//chk='';
		//for (i=0;i<scount;i++){
		//	chk=chk+ss[i];
		//	}

		document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY.value = DeAddCommaH(document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY.value);
		document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY2.value = DeAddCommaH(document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY2.value);		

		var chk=0;
		var chk4=0;
		if (trncard == '002') {
			chk = Math.round(parseFloat(document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY.value)*100)/100;
			chk4 = Math.round(parseFloat(document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY2.value)*100)/100;
			}
		else{
			chk = Math.abs(parseInt(document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY.value,10));
			chk4 = Math.abs(parseInt(document.frmbdy.TAXMONEY2.value,10));
			}			
			
		var chk3=0;
		if (trncard == '001'){
			if (document.frmbdy.hdAMT.value != ''){
				chk3 = parseInt(DeAddCommaH(document.frmbdy.hdAMT.value),10);
				}
			}
		
		document.frmbdy.RGMONEY.value = totalc - chk - chk4 - chk3;
		
		if (trncard == '002'){
			document.frmbdy.RGMONEY.value = AddCommaH(document.frmbdy.RGMONEY.value);
			}
		else{
			document.frmbdy.RGMONEY.value = AddComma(document.frmbdy.RGMONEY.value);
			}
		}	
}

//Check Length of Double Bytes Word
function checklength(fld) {
	ustr = escape(document.all(fld).value);
	nstr = document.all(fld).value;
	u = ustr.length; //Unicode Char
	n = nstr.length; //All Word
	d = (u-n)/5;	 //Double Byets Word
	e = n - d;		 //One Byte Word
	c = e + d * 2	 //Total Bytes
	n = 0;
	m = document.all(fld).maxLength;
	if (c > m){
		alert('輸入資料長度過長,部分文字將被忽略.');
		for (i=0;i < m;i++){
			ustr = escape(document.all(fld).value.substring(i,i+1));
			if (ustr.length > 1){
				n = n + 2;}
			else{
				n = n + 1;}
			if (n > m){
				i = i -1;
				break;
				}
			}
		document.all(fld).value = document.all(fld).value.substring(0,i+1);
		}
}

//Byte Substring
function BSubstr(fldstr,ss,ee) {
	n = 0;
	s = -1;
	for (i=0;i < ee;i++){
		ustr = escape(fldstr.substring(i,i+1));
		if (ustr.length > 1){
			n = n + 2;}
		else{
			n = n + 1;}
		if (n == ee){
			i = i ;
			break;
			}
		if (n > ee){
			i = i - 1;
			break;
			}

		if (n - 1 >= ss && s < 0){
			s = i;
			}
		//alert(ustr);
		}
	rc = fldstr.substring(s,i+1);
	//alert(rc);
	return rc;
}

//金額加千分位逗號
function AddCommaH(Adval) {
	var strNum = Adval;
	var lpcnt = Math.floor(strNum.length/3);
	var tempnum = '';
	
	for (i=0;i<lpcnt;i++)
		{
			tempnum = ',' + strNum.substring(strNum.length,strNum.length-3) + tempnum;
			strNum = strNum.substring(strNum.length-3,0);
		}	
	tempnum = strNum + tempnum;	

	if (tempnum.substring(0,1) == ',')
		{ tempnum = tempnum.substring(1,tempnum.length); }

	if (tempnum.substring(0,2) == '-,')
		{ tempnum = '-' + tempnum.substring(2,tempnum.length);}
		
	return tempnum;		
}

function DeAddCommaH(pThisValue) {
    if (pThisValue == '')
		{   return '';}
    i=0;
    iLen = pThisValue.length;
    while (i<iLen){ 
		tSpace = ',';
		pThisValue1 = pThisValue.replace(tSpace,'');
		if (pThisValue.length == pThisValue1.length){
			return pThisValue;
			}
		pThisValue = pThisValue1;
		i=i+1;
    }

    return pThisValue;	
}

//將數字加逗號
function AddComma(Adval) {
	//var strNum = document.all[field].value;
	var strNum = Adval;
	var lpcnt = Math.floor(strNum.length/3);
	var tempnum = '';
	
	for (i=0;i<lpcnt;i++)
		{
			tempnum = ',' + strNum.substring(strNum.length,strNum.length-3) + tempnum;
			strNum = strNum.substring(strNum.length-3,0);
		}	
	tempnum = strNum + tempnum;	

	if (tempnum.substring(0,1) == ',')
		{ tempnum = tempnum.substring(1,tempnum.length); }
		
	return tempnum;		
}

	//	return true;
    //	}
	
	else{

		}
}

//PMST營業工程款流程擷取
function SELinterComp_cal(edit_mode,A1){
	edit_md = edit_mode;
	edit_A1 = A1;
	//alert(A1);
	if ('B' != 'B' && 'B' != 'C'){
		if (frmbdy.SELTOCOMP.value == "4" || frmbdy.SELTOCOMP.value == "7"){
			if (document.frmbdy.SELACCNT.value == ''){
				document.frmbdy.SELACCNT.value = '0';
			}
			else if (parseInt(document.frmbdy.SELACCNT.value,10) <= 0){
			    document.frmbdy.SELACCNT.value = '0';
			}
			//alert(document.frmbdy.SELACCNT.value);
			//Add
			if (edit_mode == 'add'){
				if (SELinterComp_Acc(document.frmbdy.POBJNO.value,document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value) == true){
					document.frmbdy.SELACCNT.value = parseInt(document.frmbdy.SELACCNT.value,10) + 1;			
					}
				}
			//upd
			else if (edit_mode == 'upd'){
				if (SELinterComp_Acc(document.all['OBJNO' +A1].value,document.all['ITEMNO' +A1].value) == true
					&& SELinterComp_Acc(document.frmbdy.POBJNO.value,document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value) == true){
					document.frmbdy.SELACCNT.value = document.frmbdy.SELACCNT.value;
					}
				else if (SELinterComp_Acc(document.all['OBJNO' +A1].value,document.all['ITEMNO' +A1].value) == true){
					document.frmbdy.SELACCNT.value = parseInt(document.frmbdy.SELACCNT.value,10) - 1;
					}
				else if (SELinterComp_Acc(document.frmbdy.POBJNO.value,document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value) == true){
					document.frmbdy.SELACCNT.value = parseInt(document.frmbdy.SELACCNT.value,10) + 1;
					}
				}
			//del
			else if (edit_mode == 'del'){
				if (SELinterComp_Acc(document.frmbdy.POBJNO.value,document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value) == true){
					document.frmbdy.SELACCNT.value = parseInt(document.frmbdy.SELACCNT.value,10) - 1;
					}
				}
			if (parseInt(document.frmbdy.SELACCNT.value,10) > 0){
				document.all('SELinterComp').style.display = 'none';
				}
			else{
				document.all('SELinterComp').style.display = '';
			}
			//alert(document.frmbdy.SELACCNT.value);
			//SELTOCOMP_onchange('1','1A011','4X');		
			if (frmbdy.SELTOCOMP.value == "7"){
				SELTOCOMP_onchange('1','1A011','7X');
				}
			else{
				SELTOCOMP_onchange('1','1A011','4X');
				}
				
			
			}
		else {	//20180213讀取集約傳票流程
			document.all('errmsg1').innerText='流程搜尋處理中...';	
			SELTOCOMP_onchange('1','1A011','');
		}
	}
}

//流程變更
function SELTOCOMP_onchange(marea,mbugno,mareadiv){
	document.frmbdy.SELGET.disabled = false;
	//指定送件同公司別
	selarea = document.frmbdy.SELTOCOMP.value;
	if (selarea == '4'){
	    document.all('errmsg1').innerText='公司別PMST,已停止.請改用PSTW或其他.';
	    document.frmbdy.SELTOCOMP.value='';
	    document.frmbdy.SELBUGNO.value='';
	    return;
	}
	//2002/09/23 不同公司需要貸方單位
	document.frmbdy.SELBUGNO.value = trim(document.frmbdy.SELBUGNO.value.toUpperCase());
	mbugno_s = mbugno;
	if (marea == selarea && (document.frmbdy.SELBUGNO.value != '4BS03' && document.frmbdy.SELBUGNO.value != '7BS03' && document.frmbdy.SELBUGNO.value != '1B003')){
		document.frmbdy.SELBUGNO.value = '';
		}
	else if (document.frmbdy.SELBUGNO.value == ''){
		document.all('errmsg1').innerText='請填入送件單位代號.';
		document.frmbdy.SELBUGNO.focus();
		mbugno = '';
		}
	else{
		mbugno = document.frmbdy.SELBUGNO.value;
		}
	//20180213 取第0筆(零)
	//alert(document.form2.selRow.options[0].value);
	//alert(document.frmbdy.oSpacnt.value);
	A1=document.form2.selRow.options[0].value
	ActCnt = 12 - parseInt(document.frmbdy.oSpacnt.value,10);
	if (edit_md=="del" && ActCnt != 0)
		ActCnt = ActCnt-1;
	//alert(ActCnt);
	ActCenterurl="";
	if (edit_md=="del" && edit_A1 == A1 && ActCnt == 1)
		A1=document.form2.selRow.options[1].value;
	if (edit_md=="del") {
		ActCenterurl = '&ACTNO1='+document.all("OBJNO"+A1).value+'&ACTITNO='+document.all("ITEMNO"+A1).value;
		}
	else if (ActCnt !=0) {
		ActCenterurl = '&ACTNO1='+document.frmbdy.POBJNO.value+'&ACTITNO='+document.frmbdy.PITEMNO.value;
		if (document.frmbdy.POBJNO.value=="" && document.all("OBJNO"+A1).value !="")
			ActCenterurl = '&ACTNO1='+document.all("OBJNO"+A1).value+'&ACTITNO='+document.all("ITEMNO"+A1).value;
		}
	ActCenterurl = ActCenterurl + "&ActCenterNow=" + document.frmbdy.ActCenter.value + "&ActCnt=" + ActCnt;
	
	ActCenterurl = ActCenterurl + "&manno=" + document.frmbdy.hdMANNO.value;
	
	//alert(ActCenterurl);
	//流程搜尋
	if (parseInt(document.frmbdy.SELACCNT.value,10) > 0){//20100604 PMST特別科目窗口債權監理
		document.all('errmsg1').innerText='流程搜尋處理中...';
		parent.frames['FIND'].location.href = 'PEPH6102.asp?ACTION=flowget&selarea=' + mareadiv.substring(0,1) + '&selbugdiv=' + mareadiv.substring(1,2) + ActCenterurl+'&T='+'20260126113634';
		}
	else if ((mbugno != '' && mareadiv == '') || (parseInt(document.frmbdy.SELACCNT.value,10) <= 0)){
		document.all('errmsg1').innerText='流程搜尋處理中...';
		window.document.all('flowstring').innerHTML = '';
		//20180607 PMST取消 跨公司窗口,改各監理
		//if (selarea == '4' && selarea != marea && mbugno.substring(0,1) != 'S' && mbugno.substring(0,1) != 'D'){
		//	selbugdiv = '0'	//PMST 跨公司窗口本社監理
	    //	parent.frames['FIND'].location.href = 'PEPH6102.asp?ACTION=flowget&selarea=' + selarea +  '&selbugdiv=' + selbugdiv + ActCenterurl+'&T='+'20260126113634';
		//	}
		//else{ //其他 跨公司
		parent.frames['FIND'].location.href = 'PEPH6102.asp?ACTION=flowget&selarea=' + selarea +  '&selbugno=' + mbugno + ActCenterurl+'&T='+'20260126113634';
		//	}
		}
	//送件單位
	if (document.frmbdy.SELBUGNO.value == ''){
		document.frmbdy.APPBUG.value = trim(mbugno);
		}
	else if (marea == selarea && (document.frmbdy.SELBUGNO.value == '4BS03' || document.frmbdy.SELBUGNO.value == '7BS03' || document.frmbdy.SELBUGNO.value == '1B003')){
		document.frmbdy.APPBUG.value = trim(mbugno_s);
		}
	else{
		document.frmbdy.APPBUG.value = trim(document.frmbdy.SELBUGNO.value);
		}
	if (trncard == '003'){
		document.frmbdy.hdDept.value = trim(document.frmbdy.APPBUG.value);
		}		
}

function PreSELTOCOMP_onchange(marea,mbugno,mareadiv){
	//Clear Data
	parent.frames['ITM'].location.href = 'PEPH6105.ASP';
	parent.frames['BUG'].location.href = 'PEPH6107.ASP';
	if (trncard == '001'){
		document.frmbdy.hdMANNO.value = '';
		hdMANNO_onblur();
		}
	else if (trncard == '002'){
		document.frmbdy.hdACCNO.value = '';
		hdACCNO_onblur();
		document.frmbdy.selBKCU.options[0].selected = true;
		selBKCU_onchange();
		parent.frames['VHR'].location.href = 'PEPH6134.ASP';
		}
	else if (trncard == '003'){
		document.frmbdy.selVHRTYPE.options[0].selected = true;
		selVHRTYPE_onchange();
		}
	SELTOCOMP_onchange(marea,mbugno,mareadiv);
}

//**受款人各欄檢查函式開始**********************
function hdMANNO_onkeyup() {
	document.all('errmsg1').innerText='';
	var objchk=document.frmbdy.hdMANNO.value;
	document.frmbdy.hdTMPNO.readOnly = true;
	if (objchk.length==10){
		document.frmbdy.POBJNO.focus();
		}
}

function hdMANNO_onfocus() {	
	document.all('errmsg1').innerText='說明:受款人代號是員工代號、廠商統一編號或個人的身分證字號.';
}

function hdMANNO_onblur() {
	document.all('errmsg1').innerText='';
	if (document.frmbdy.hdMANNO.value=='' && document.frmbdy.hdMANNA.value==''){
		return;
		}
	var chk=document.frmbdy.hdMANNO.value;
	document.frmbdy.hdMANNA.value='';	
	document.frmbdy.hdCrActNo.value = '';
	document.frmbdy.hdCrItmNo.value = '';
	document.frmbdy.hdCrActN1.value = '';
	document.frmbdy.hdCrItmN1.value = '';
	document.frmbdy.hdBankNo.value = '';
	document.frmbdy.hdBranch.value = '';
	document.frmbdy.hdCountNo.value = '';
	document.frmbdy.hdCOUNTNAME.value = '';
		
	document.frmbdy.hdTMPNO.value = '';
	document.frmbdy.hdAMT.value='';
	document.frmbdy.hdTMPNO1.value = '';
	document.frmbdy.hdAMT1.value='';
	document.frmbdy.hdTMPNO2.value = '';
	document.frmbdy.hdAMT2.value='';
	document.frmbdy.hdTMPNO3.value = '';
	document.frmbdy.hdAMT3.value='';
	document.frmbdy.hdTMPNO4.value = '';
	document.frmbdy.hdAMT4.value='';
	document.frmbdy.hdTMPNO5.value = '';
	document.frmbdy.hdAMT5.value='';
	
	if 	(chk.substring(0,1)==' '){
		document.frmbdy.hdMANNO.value='';
		alert('受款人代號不可空白');
		document.frmbdy.hdMANNO.focus();
		return;
		}
	document.frmbdy.hdMANNO.value = document.frmbdy.hdMANNO.value.toUpperCase();
	var actno = document.frmbdy.hdMANNO.value;
	parent.frames['FIND'].location.href = 'PEPH6102.asp?ACTION=mannoget&ACTNO1=' + actno  + '&BUGAREA=' + parent.frames['mail'].frmbdy.SELTOCOMP.value +'&T='+'20260126113634';
}

function hdVHRCNT_onblur() {
	
	var chk=document.frmbdy.hdVHRCNT.value;
	
	if 	(chk.substring(0,1)==''){
		return;
		}	
	if 	(chk.substring(0,1)==' '){
		document.frmbdy.hdVHRCNT.value='';
		return;
		}	

	document.frmbdy.hdVHRCNT.value=Math.abs(parseInt(document.frmbdy.hdVHRCNT.value,10));
	//alert(document.frmbdy.hdVHRCNT.value);
	//alert(VHRdatain.rows.length);
	//Add Rows
	for (hi = VHRdatain.rows.length; document.frmbdy.hdVHRCNT.value < VHRdatain.rows.length; hi--){
		VHRdatain.deleteRow(hi-1);
		}
//alert("b");	
	for (i = 0; document.frmbdy.hdVHRCNT.value > VHRdatain.rows.length ; i++){
//alert("c");	
		var rowcnt = VHRdatain.rows.length;
		var addcnt = rowcnt + 1;
		VHRdatain.insertRow();	
		VHRdatain.rows[rowcnt].align = 'center';
	
		for (icount = 0; icount < 10 ; icount++ ){
			VHRdatain.rows[rowcnt].insertCell();
			}

		//var a = '<INPUT TYPE=HIDDEN id=redebno' + addcnt + ' name=redebno' + addcnt + ' size=12 MAXLENGTH=12 style="text-align: center">';
		//var aElement=document.createElement(a);
		//VHRdatain.rows[rowcnt].cells[0].insertAdjacentHTML('beforeEnd',a);
		var a = document.createElement("input");
		a.type = "text";
		a.name = "redebno"+ addcnt;
		a.id = "redebno"+ addcnt;
		a.style.width="100%";
		a.style.border="none";
		a.style.textAlign="center";
		a.value = "";
		a.readOnly = true;
		VHRdatain.rows[rowcnt].cells[0].appendChild(a);

		var a = document.createElement("input");

		a.style.border="none";
		a.style.textAlign="right";
		a.value = "";
		a.readOnly = true;
		VHRdatain.rows[rowcnt].cells[6].appendChild(a);

		//var a = '<INPUT TYPE=HIDDEN id=redept' + addcnt + ' name=redept' + addcnt + ' size=8 MAXLENGTH=8 style="text-align: right">';
		//var aElement=document.createElement(a);
		//VHRdatain.rows[rowcnt].cells[5].insertAdjacentHTML('beforeEnd',a);
		var a = document.createElement("input");
		a.type = "text";
		a.name = "redept"+ addcnt;
		a.id = "redept"+ addcnt;
		a.style.width="100%";
		a.style.border="none";
		a.style.textAlign="right";
		a.value = "";
		a.readOnly = true;
		VHRdatain.rows[rowcnt].cells[7].appendChild(a);



		//var a = '<INPUT TYPE=HIDDEN id=rectno' + addcnt + ' name=rectno' + addcnt + ' size=11 MAXLENGTH=11 style="text-align: center">';
		//var aElement=document.createElement(a);
		//VHRdatain.rows[rowcnt].cells[7].insertAdjacentHTML('beforeEnd',a);
		var a = document.createElement("input");
		a.type = "text";
		a.name = "rectno"+ addcnt;
		a.id = "rectno"+ addcnt;
		a.style.width="100%";
		a.style.border="none";
		a.style.textAlign="center";
		a.value = "";
		a.readOnly = true;
		VHRdatain.rows[rowcnt].cells[8].appendChild(a);
	
		//var a = '<INPUT TYPE=HIDDEN id=redivname' + addcnt + ' name=redivname' + addcnt + ' size=6 MAXLENGTH=6 style="border:none;text-align: center" readonly>';
		//var aElement=document.createElement(a);
		//VHRdatain.rows[rowcnt].cells[8].insertAdjacentHTML('beforeEnd',a);
		var a = document.createElement("input");
		a.type = "text";
		a.name = "redivname"+ addcnt;
		a.id = "redivname"+ addcnt;
		a.style.width="100%";
		a.style.border="none";
		a.style.textAlign="center";
		a.value = "";
		a.readOnly = true;
		VHRdatain.rows[rowcnt].cells[9].appendChild(a);
		
	}
//alert("ccc");	
}

var intSel = 0;
var strSobj = '';
function btndel_onclick() {
	if (intSel < 0 || strSobj == ''){
		document.all('spninmsg').innerText='請點選要刪除的一筆資料.';
		return;
		}
	for (i=0 ; i<document.frmbdy[strSobj].length ; i++){
		if(document.frmbdy[strSobj].options[i].selected == true){
			//alert(i);
		document.all('spninmsg').innerText='請點選要刪除的一筆資料.';
		return;
			}
		}
		
	if (intSel < 0 || strSobj == ''){
		document.all('spninmsg').innerText='請點選要刪除的一筆資料.';
		return;
		}
	
	//1.Update Debit Amount must equal to Total Credit Amount
	frmbdy.txtsum.value = parseFloat(DeAddCommaH(frmbdy.txtsum.value)) - parseFloat(frmbdy.hidinamt.value);
	frmbdy.txtsum.value = AddCommaH(frmbdy.txtsum.value);
	frmbdy.taxsum.value = parseFloat(DeAddCommaH(frmbdy.taxsum.value)) - parseFloat(frmbdy.hidintax.value);
	frmbdy.taxsum.value = AddCommaH(frmbdy.taxsum.value);
	frmbdy.txtcnt.value = parseFloat(DeAddCommaH(frmbdy.txtcnt.value)) - 1;
	
	//3.Delete Option in Visible Select Object
	document.frmbdy[strSobj].remove(intSel);
	
	//6.Clear Edit Text In Input Object
	clear_sel();

	//7.Move Bookmark To Next If Option Exist
	if (document.frmbdy[strSobj].length == 0){
		intSel = -1;
		}
	else if (intSel > document.frmbdy[strSobj].length - 1){
		intSel = -1;
		}
	else{
		document.frmbdy[strSobj].options[intSel].selected = true;
		sel_gv(strSobj);
		}
		
	//8.Show Msg
	parent.frames['FIND'].location.href = 'peph6102.asp?action=chkdel';
}

function btnadd_onclick(DOCN,trncard) {
	//0.Check Validate Value
	frmbdy.UNITIVEND.value = frmbdy.UNITIVEND.value.toUpperCase();
	if (chk_in_v('a') == false){
		strSobj = '';
		return};
	document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:檢查中,請稍後..';
	document.all('errmsg1').innerText='';
	
	strSobj = 'selindata1';

	// ELECINVO=document.frmbdy.ELECINVO.value;
	// CHKIND=document.frmbdy.CHKIND.value;
	// if (ELECINVO !='' && CHKIND !='0'){
	// 	alert("電子發票廠商發票類別為0，不可使用其他發票類別請款！");
	// }
		
	//Check All Doc
	strURL = 'peph6102.asp?action=chkadd&intSel=' + intSel + '&sel=' + strSobj
	strURL = strURL + '&ck=' + frmbdy.CHKIND.value;
	strURL = strURL + '&ve=' + frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.value;
	strURL = strURL + '&ym=' + frmbdy.YYYYMM.value;
	strURL = strURL + '&un=' + frmbdy.UNITIVEND.value
	strURL = strURL + '&am=' + DeAddCommaH(frmbdy.AMT.value);
	strURL = strURL + '&tm=' + DeAddCommaH(frmbdy.TAXAMT.value);
	strURL = strURL + '&cn=' + frmbdy.CHCNT.value;
	strURL = strURL + '&td=' + trncard;
	strURL = strURL + '&N5ABC=' + 'N';
	try{bugarea=parent.frames['mail'].frmbdy.SELTOCOMP.value;}
		catch(e){bugarea='1';}
	strURL = strURL + '&bugarea=' + bugarea;
	try{strURL = strURL + '&txtmon2=' + frmbdy.txtmon2.value;}
		catch(e){}
	strURL = strURL + '&dt=' + TimeDemo();
	strSobj = '';
	document.frmbdy.CHKIND.focus();
	parent.frames['FIND'].location.href = strURL;
}
