	//0.Check Validate Value
	if (intSel < 0 || strSobj == ''){

	frmbdy.UNITIVEND.value = frmbdy.UNITIVEND.value.toUpperCase();
	if (chk_in_v('u') == false || intSel < 0){

	document.all('errmsg1').innerText='';
	strURL = 'peph6102.asp?action=chkupd&intSel=' + intSel + '&sel=' + strSobj;
	strURL = strURL + '&ck=' + frmbdy.CHKIND.value;
	strURL = strURL + '&ve=' + frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.value;
	strURL = strURL + '&ym=' + frmbdy.YYYYMM.value;
	strURL = strURL + '&un=' + frmbdy.UNITIVEND.value
	strURL = strURL + '&am=' + DeAddCommaH(frmbdy.AMT.value);
	strURL = strURL + '&tm=' + DeAddCommaH(frmbdy.TAXAMT.value);
	strURL = strURL + '&cn=' + frmbdy.CHCNT.value;
	strURL = strURL + '&td=' + trncard;
	strURL = strURL + '&N5ABC=' + 'N';
	try{bugarea=parent.frames['mail'].frmbdy.SELTOCOMP.value;}
		catch(e){bugarea='1';}
	strURL = strURL + '&bugarea=' + bugarea;
	try{strURL = strURL + '&txtmon2=' + frmbdy.txtmon2.value;}

	strURL = strURL + '&dt=' + TimeDemo();

	document.frmbdy.CHKIND.focus();

}

//Check In-Value
function chk_in_v(act) {
	str1 = '0123456789';
	strc = str1.indexOf(frmbdy.CHKIND.value)
	if (strc < 0 || frmbdy.CHKIND.value == ''){
		document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:發票類別是0到9!';
		frmbdy.CHKIND.focus();
		return false;}

	if (strc == 0 || strc == 1 || strc == 2 || strc == 6 || strc == 9){
	 	if (frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.value.length != 8){
			document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:廠商統編是8位!';
			frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.focus();
			return false;}
			
		if (Chk_IDNO(frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.value) == false){		
			document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:廠商統編錯誤!';
			frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.focus();
			return false;}
					
		if (frmbdy.UNITIVEND.value.length != 10){
			document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:統一發票號碼是10位!';
			frmbdy.UNITIVEND.focus();
			return false;}
			
		tmpstr = "1." + frmbdy.UNITIVEND.value.substring(2,10);
		if (parseFloat(tmpstr)/1 != tmpstr){
		//if (tmpstr.toLowerCase() != tmpstr.toUpperCase()){
			document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:統一發票後8碼是數字!';
			frmbdy.UNITIVEND.focus();
			return false;}
		}
	else if (strc == 4 || strc == 7){
	 	if (frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.value.length != 8){
			document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:廠商統編是8位!';
			frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.focus();
			return false;}
			
		if (Chk_IDNO(frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.value) == false){		
			document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:廠商統編錯誤!';
			frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.focus();
			return false;}
			
		
		if (parseFloat(frmbdy.TAXAMT.value) == 0 && strc == 4){
			document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:稅額不能等於零!';
			frmbdy.TAXAMT.focus();
			return false;}

		if (parseFloat(frmbdy.AMT.value) >= 0 && strc == 7){
			document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:金額不能大於零!';
			frmbdy.TAXAMT.focus();
			return false;}

		if (frmbdy.UNITIVEND.value.length != 10){
			document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:統一發票號碼是10位!';
			frmbdy.UNITIVEND.focus();
			return false;}
			
		tmpstr = "1." + frmbdy.UNITIVEND.value.substring(2,10);
		if (parseFloat(tmpstr)/1 != tmpstr){
		//if (tmpstr.toLowerCase() != tmpstr.toUpperCase()){
			document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:統一發票後8碼是數字!';
			frmbdy.UNITIVEND.focus();
			return false;}
				
		}
	else if (strc == 5 || strc == 8){
		frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.value = '';
		if (frmbdy.YYYYMM.value.length != 4 && frmbdy.YYYYMM.value.length != 5){//20100928
			document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:年月是4~5位!';
			frmbdy.YYYYMM.focus();
			return false;}

		if (frmbdy.UNITIVEND.value.length != 14){
			document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:稅單號碼是14位!';
			frmbdy.UNITIVEND.focus();
			return false;}		
		tmpstr = frmbdy.UNITIVEND.value.substring(0,3).toUpperCase() ;
		
		//第5類字首3碼大部分是英文字20030711
		
		if (tmpstr.substring(0,1) < 'A' || tmpstr.substring(0,1) > 'Z'){
			document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:稅單號碼字首第一碼是英文字!';
			frmbdy.UNITIVEND.focus();
			return false;}		

		if (tmpstr.substring(1,2) < 'A' || tmpstr.substring(1,2) > 'Z'){
			document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:稅單號碼字首第二碼是英文字!';
			frmbdy.UNITIVEND.focus();
			return false;}		

		if (tmpstr.substring(2,3) < 'A' || tmpstr.substring(2,3) > 'Z'){
			document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:稅單號碼字首第三碼是英文字!';
			frmbdy.UNITIVEND.focus();
			return false;}
		//20180125
		//tmpstr = frmbdy.UNITIVEND.value.substring(3,14);
		//if (tmpstr.toLowerCase() != tmpstr.toUpperCase()){
		//	document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:稅單號碼不正確!';
		//	frmbdy.UNITIVEND.focus();
		//	return false;}
				
		//***		
		}
	else if (strc == 3){
		//window.alert(event.srcElement.id);
		//if (event.srcElement.id == 'btnnew'){
			for(i3 = 0; i3 < document.frmbdy['selindata1'].length;i3++){
				ss = document.frmbdy['selindata1'].options[i3].text.split(';')
				if (ss.length < 3) break
				//window.alert(ss[0] + frmbdy.CHKIND.value + trim(ss[1]) + frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.value +  trim(ss[6]) + document.frmbdy.CHCNT.value);
				if (ss[0] == frmbdy.CHKIND.value && trim(ss[1]) == '' && frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.value=='' && trim(ss[6]) != '' && document.frmbdy.CHCNT.value != ''){
					document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:發票類別' + frmbdy.CHKIND.value + '請彙總張數為一筆!';
					//window.alert(act+intSel+i3)					
					if (act =='a'){
						return false;
						}
					if (intSel != i3){
						return false;
						}
					}
				}
			//}
		if (document.frmbdy.CHCNT.value != ""){
			if (parseInt(frmbdy.CHCNT.value,10)/1 == frmbdy.CHCNT.value){
				frmbdy.CHCNT.value = parseFloat(frmbdy.CHCNT.value);}
			else{
				document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:單筆500元以下,需登錄張數,或501元以上,不需張數!';
				return false;}
			}
		if (document.frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.value==""){
			if (parseInt(frmbdy.CHCNT.value,10)/1 != frmbdy.CHCNT.value && Math.abs(parseFloat(frmbdy.TAXAMT.value)) <= 500){
				document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:請登錄憑證張數!';
				frmbdy.CHCNT.focus();
				return false;}				
			if (trim(frmbdy.CHCNT.value) == "" && Math.abs(parseFloat(frmbdy.TAXAMT.value)) >= 501){
				document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:第三類稅額單筆501元以上,需登錄統編!';
				frmbdy.CHCNT.focus();
				return false;}
			if (frmbdy.CHCNT.value == "1" && Math.abs(parseFloat(frmbdy.TAXAMT.value)) >= 501){
				document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:單筆501元以上,不需登錄張數,需登錄統編!';
				frmbdy.CHCNT.focus();
				return false;}
			}
		else{
			if (Math.abs(parseFloat(frmbdy.TAXAMT.value)) <= 500){
				document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:第三類稅額500元以下,請合併成1筆,不需登錄統編!';
				frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.focus();
				return false;}
			if (Chk_IDNO(frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.value) == false){		
				document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:廠商統編錯誤!';
				frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.focus();
				return false;}
			if (frmbdy.CHCNT.value != ""){
				document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:輸入統編後,憑證張數不需登錄,請清除空白!';
				frmbdy.CHCNT.focus();
				return false;}
			}
		if (parseFloat(frmbdy.CHCNT.value) <= 0 && frmbdy.TAXAMT.value.substring(0,1) != '-'){
			document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:稅額正數,憑證張數請輸入正數!';
			frmbdy.CHCNT.focus();
			return false;}
		if (parseFloat(frmbdy.CHCNT.value) >= 0 && frmbdy.TAXAMT.value.substring(0,1) == '-'){
			document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:稅額負數,憑證張數請輸入負數!';
			frmbdy.CHCNT.focus();
			return false;}
		
		frmbdy.YYYYMM.value     = '';
		frmbdy.UNITIVEND.value  = '';		
		}


	//check This Doc
	if (strc != 3){
		re = /\xA0/g;
		frmbdy.CHCNT.value = '';
		for(dupi=0;dupi<document.frmbdy['selindata1'].length;dupi++){
			ss = document.frmbdy['selindata1'].options[dupi].text.split(';')
			if (ss.length < 3) break			
			ss[3] = ss[3].replace(re,"");
			
			if (trim(ss[3]) == frmbdy.UNITIVEND.value){
				if (window.confirm('此發票號碼重複!確定?') == false){
					return false;
					}
				}

			if (trim(ss[3]) == frmbdy.UNITIVEND.value && ss[0] == frmbdy.CHKIND.value){
				if (act == 'u' && strSobj == 'selindata1' && intSel == dupi){
					act = act;
					}
				else{
					document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:' + frmbdy.UNITIVEND.value + '類別及發票號碼重複!';
					return false;
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
	if (strc == 5 || strc == 8){
		//check YYYYMM
		d = new Date();
		YYYYMM1 = d.getFullYear() - 1911;//Year
		YYYYMM2 = d.getMonth() + 1;//Month
		YYYYMMd = YYYYMM2 / 2 ;
		if (YYYYMMd != parseInt(YYYYMMd,10)){
			YYYYMMU = YYYYMM2 + 1;
			YYYYMM2 = YYYYMM2 - 2;
			//alert('aYYYYMM1=' + YYYYMM1 + 'YYYYMM2=' + YYYYMM2+ 'YYYYMMU=' + YYYYMMU);
			}
		else{
			YYYYMMU = YYYYMM2;
			YYYYMM2 = YYYYMM2 - 3;
			//alert('bYYYYMM1=' + YYYYMM1 + 'YYYYMM2=' + YYYYMM2+ 'YYYYMMU=' + YYYYMMU);
			}
		if (YYYYMM2 < 0){
			YYYYMM2 = 12 + YYYYMM2;
			YYYYMM1 = YYYYMM1 - 1;
			//alert('cYYYYMM1=' + YYYYMM1 + 'YYYYMM2=' + YYYYMM2);
			}
		YYYYMM2 = YYYYMM2 + 100;//Month
		YYYYMMU = YYYYMMU + 100;//Month
		YYYYMM2 = YYYYMM2.toString();//Month
		YYYYMMU = YYYYMMU.toString();//Month
		YYYYMML = YYYYMM1 + '' + YYYYMM2.substring(1,3);//Year+Month
		//YYYYMMU = '97' + '' + YYYYMMU.substring(1,3);
		YYYYMMU = parseInt((d.getFullYear() + '' + YYYYMMU.substring(1,3)),10)-191100;	//20080107//Year+Month
		YYYYMMAdd = 0;
		if (d.getFullYear() - 1911 >= 100 && parseInt(frmbdy.YYYYMM.value.substring(0,2),10) < 10){//20100928
			YYYYMMAdd = 10000;
			}
		
		if (YYYYMMAdd + parseInt(frmbdy.YYYYMM.value,10) < parseInt(YYYYMML,10)){
			document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:發票年月最小是' + YYYYMML + '!';
			return false;
			}
		
		if (YYYYMMAdd + parseInt(frmbdy.YYYYMM.value,10) > parseInt(YYYYMMU,10) && '1A011' != 'I61'){
			document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:發票年月最大是' + YYYYMMU + '!';
			return false;
			}
		if (frmbdy.YYYYMM.value.length != 4 && frmbdy.YYYYMM.value.length != 5){
			document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:發票年月是4~5位!';
			frmbdy.YYYYMM.focus();
			return false;}
		//20100928增加check年月5碼
		chkval= frmbdy.YYYYMM.value.substring(frmbdy.YYYYMM.value.length-2,frmbdy.YYYYMM.value.length);
		if (chkval < '01' || chkval > '12'){
			document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:[' + chkval + ']錯誤,發票月份是01~12!';
			frmbdy.YYYYMM.focus();
			return false;}
		if (parseFloat(frmbdy.YYYYMM.value) != frmbdy.YYYYMM.value){
			document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:[' + frmbdy.YYYYMM.value + ']錯誤,發票年月是數字!';
			frmbdy.YYYYMM.focus();
			return false;}
		chkval= frmbdy.YYYYMM.value.substring(0,1);
		if (parseFloat(chkval) != chkval || chkval == 0 || chkval < 0 || chkval > 9){
			document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:年月第1碼[' + chkval + ']錯誤,發票年月是數字!';
			frmbdy.YYYYMM.focus();
			return false;}
		chkval= frmbdy.YYYYMM.value.substring(1,2);
		if (parseFloat(chkval) != chkval || chkval < 0 || chkval > 9){
			document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:年月第2碼[' + chkval + ']錯誤,發票年月是數字!';
			frmbdy.YYYYMM.focus();
			return false;}
		chkval= frmbdy.YYYYMM.value.substring(2,3);
		if (parseFloat(chkval) != chkval || chkval < 0 || chkval > 9){
			document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:年月第3碼[' + chkval + ']錯誤,發票年月是數字!';
			frmbdy.YYYYMM.focus();
			return false;}
		}

	tot = parseFloat(DeAddCommaH(frmbdy.txtsum.value)) + parseFloat(frmbdy.AMT.value);
	if (tot.toString().length > 11){
		document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:金額長度是11位!';
		return false;}

	tot = parseFloat(DeAddCommaH(frmbdy.taxsum.value)) + parseFloat(frmbdy.TAXAMT.value);
	if (tot.toString().length > 10){
		document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:稅額長度是10位!';
		return false;}
		
	if (parseInt(frmbdy.AMT.value,10)/1 != frmbdy.AMT.value || parseFloat(frmbdy.AMT.value) == 0){
		document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:金額是整數!';
		frmbdy.AMT.focus();
		return false;}
	frmbdy.AMT.value = parseFloat(frmbdy.AMT.value);

	//if (parseInt(frmbdy.TAXAMT.value,10)/1 != frmbdy.TAXAMT.value || parseFloat(frmbdy.TAXAMT.value) < 0){
	if (parseInt(frmbdy.TAXAMT.value,10)/1 != frmbdy.TAXAMT.value){
		document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:稅額是整數!';
		frmbdy.TAXAMT.focus();
		return false;}

	if (parseFloat(frmbdy.AMT.value) >= 0 && parseFloat(frmbdy.TAXAMT.value) < 0){
		document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:金額正數,稅額請輸入正整數!';
		frmbdy.TAXAMT.focus();
		return false;}

	if (parseFloat(frmbdy.AMT.value) < 0 && parseFloat(frmbdy.TAXAMT.value) > 0){
		document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:金額負數,稅額請輸入負數!';
		frmbdy.TAXAMT.focus();
		return false;}
	
	if (strc != 5 && strc != 6 && strc != 7 && strc != 8 && strc != 9 && Math.abs(parseFloat(frmbdy.TAXAMT.value) - Math.round(document.frmbdy.AMT.value / 1.05 * 0.05)) >= 5){
		document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:5類、8類和9類以外,稅額計算誤差必須小於5!';
		frmbdy.TAXAMT.focus();
		return false;}
	
	frmbdy.TAXAMT.value = parseFloat(frmbdy.TAXAMT.value);
	frmbdy.UNITIVEND.value = frmbdy.UNITIVEND.value.toUpperCase();
	return true;
}

function trim(pThisValue){
    var tSpace,ixI;
    pThisValue = pThisValue.toString();
    if (pThisValue == "")
    {   return "";}
    i=0;
    iLen =  pThisValue.length;
    re = /\xA0/g;
    while (i<iLen){ 
      tSpace = " ";
      pThisValue = pThisValue.replace(tSpace,"");
      pThisValue = pThisValue.replace(re,"");
      i=i+1;
    }

    return pThisValue;
}

function checkspec(repl){
	var r, re;                    //Declare variables.
	var ss = repl.value;
	if (trim(repl.value) == '') {
		return;
		} 
	re = /[\x22\x27\x5c\x26\x23\x3c\x3d\x3e\x3f\x7b\x7d]/g;
	r = ss.replace(re, "~");
	re = "--";
	r = r.replace(re, "~~");
	re = "/*";
	r = r.replace(re, "~~");
	re = "*/";
	r = r.replace(re, "~~");
	repl.value=r;
}


var intSel
var strSobj
//Select object
function selindata_onclick(evtobj,strmd,strcf,strSt) {
	if (((strmd == '99' || strmd == '97') && strcf != 'Y') || (strSt != 'B' && strSt != 'C')){
		currentTab = evtobj; //window.event.srcElement;
		//功能列按鈕id
		if (typeof(currentTab) != "object" || currentTab == null)//IE ERR
		{
			return;
		}
		if (typeof(currentTab.id) == 'undefined' )//CHROME ERR
		{
			return;
		}
		//alert(currentTab.selectedIndex);
		
		try{intSel = currentTab.selectedIndex;}catch(e){}
		if (intSel >= 0) sel_gv(currentTab.id);
		}
	else{
		currentTab.selectedIndex = -1;
		}
	}

function sc(s,n){
	j = s.length;
	for (i=n ;i > j ;i--){
		//s = '&nbsp;' + s;
		//Because '&nbsp;' is Html,IE5.0 Not support innerHtml,Must Use ASCII Code To Insert Text
		s = String.fromCharCode(0xA0) + s;
		}
	return s;
}

function sel_gv(selid) {
	s  = document.frmbdy[selid].options[intSel].text;	
	document.frmbdy[selid].selectedIndex = -1;
	if (s.indexOf(';') > 0){
		ss = s.split(';');
		re = /\xA0/g;
		ss[1] = ss[1].replace(re,"");
		ss[2] = ss[2].replace(re,"");
		ss[3] = ss[3].replace(re,"");
		ss[4] = ss[4].replace(re,"");
		ss[5] = ss[5].replace(re,"");
		ss[6] = ss[6].replace(re,"");
		
		frmbdy.CHKIND.value		 = ss[0];
		frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.value = trim(ss[1]);
		frmbdy.YYYYMM.value		 = trim(ss[2]);
		frmbdy.UNITIVEND.value	 = trim(ss[3]);
		frmbdy.AMT.value		 = parseFloat(ss[4]);
		frmbdy.TAXAMT.value		 = parseFloat(ss[5]);
		frmbdy.CHCNT.value		 = trim(ss[6]);

		frmbdy.hidinamt.value	 = parseFloat(ss[4]);
		frmbdy.hidintax.value	 = parseFloat(ss[5]);
			
		strSobj = selid;
		document.all("spninmsg").innerText = "";
		chg_spnT(ss[0]);
		CHKIND_onkeyup();
		}
	else{
		clear_sel();
		strSobj = '';
		intSel = - 1;
		}
	}

		document.all('spnT1').style.display = '';
		document.all('spnT2').style.display = 'none';
		document.all('spnT3')[0].style.display = 'none';
		}

		document.all("spnAtaxCD2").innerText = '2302-3#03';

		}
	else {

		document.all("spnAtaxCD2").innerText = '2302-3#03';
		document.all('spnT3')[0].innerText = '發票號碼';

		document.all('spnT3')[1].innerText = '發票號碼';

		document.all('spnT1').style.display = '';

function clear_sel() {
	frmbdy.CHKIND.value		 = '';
	frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.value = '';
	frmbdy.YYYYMM.value		 = '';
	frmbdy.UNITIVEND.value	 = '';
	frmbdy.AMT.value		 = '';
	frmbdy.TAXAMT.value		 = '';
	frmbdy.CHCNT.value		 = '';
	}

function CHKIND_onkeyup() {
	var objchk=frmbdy.CHKIND.value;
	var ITMID= 20;
	var PAYLENG = 0;
	if (ITMID == 15){
		var PAYTYPE = 1;
	}else if (ITMID == 20 || ITMID == 25){
		var PAYTYPE = parent.frames['mail'].document.frmbdy.PAYTYPE.value;
		if (parent.frames['mail'] && parent.frames['mail'].document.frmbdy && parent.frames['mail'].document.frmbdy.hdMANNO !== undefined) {
			var PAYLENG = parent.frames['mail'].document.frmbdy.hdMANNO.value.length; //判斷台幣電匯受款人長度是否為6員工
		}
	}else{
		var PAYTYPE = 2;
	}

	if (objchk=='6' || objchk=='7'){
		document.frmbdy.TAXAMT.readOnly = true;
		}
	else{
		document.frmbdy.TAXAMT.readOnly = false;
		}

	if (objchk=='0'){
		if (PAYTYPE == 1 || PAYLENG == 6 ){ //員工代墊可手打及選用 //轉帳傳票
			document.frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.disabled = false;
			document.frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.focus();
			document.frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.style.border = 'silver 1px inset';
			document.frmbdy.YYYYMM.style.border = 'silver 1px inset';
			document.frmbdy.YYYYMM.disabled = false;
			document.frmbdy.UNITIVEND.disabled = false;
			document.frmbdy.AMT.disabled = false;
			document.frmbdy.TAXAMT.disabled = false;
		}else{
			document.frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.disabled = false;
			document.frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.focus();
			document.frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.style.border = 'silver 1px inset';
			document.frmbdy.YYYYMM.style.border = 'silver 1px inset';
			document.frmbdy.YYYYMM.disabled = true;
			document.frmbdy.UNITIVEND.disabled=true;
			document.frmbdy.AMT.disabled = true;
			document.frmbdy.TAXAMT.disabled = true;
			document.frmbdy.YYYYMM.value = '';
			document.frmbdy.UNITIVEND.value = '';
			document.frmbdy.AMT.value = '';
			document.frmbdy.TAXAMT.value = '';
		}
		document.frmbdy.UNITIVEND.style.border = 'silver 1px inset';
		document.frmbdy.CHCNT.disabled = true;
		document.frmbdy.CHCNT.value = '';
		document.all('spninmsg').innerText='';
		//document.frmbdy.btneinvoice.style.visibility = 'visible';
        document.frmbdy.btneinvoice.removeAttribute("disabled");
		}
	else if (objchk=='1' || objchk=='2' || objchk=='6'){
		document.frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.disabled = false;
		document.frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.focus();
		document.frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.style.border = 'silver 1px inset';
		document.frmbdy.YYYYMM.disabled = false; //20131227
		//document.frmbdy.YYYYMM.value=''; //20131227
		document.frmbdy.YYYYMM.style.border = 'silver 1px inset'; //20131227
		document.frmbdy.UNITIVEND.disabled=false;
		document.frmbdy.UNITIVEND.style.border = 'silver 1px inset';
		document.frmbdy.AMT.disabled=false;
		document.frmbdy.TAXAMT.disabled=false;
		document.frmbdy.CHCNT.disabled = true;
		document.frmbdy.CHCNT.value = '';
		document.all('spninmsg').innerText='';
		// document.frmbdy.btneinvoice.style.visibility = 'hidden';
		document.frmbdy.btneinvoice.setAttribute("disabled", "disabled");
		}
	else if (objchk=='4' || objchk=='7'){
		document.frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.disabled = false;
		document.frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.focus();
		document.frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.style.border = 'silver 1px inset';
		
		document.frmbdy.YYYYMM.disabled = true;
		document.frmbdy.YYYYMM.value='';
		document.frmbdy.YYYYMM.style.border = 'none';
		
		document.frmbdy.UNITIVEND.disabled=false;
		document.frmbdy.UNITIVEND.style.border = 'silver 1px inset';
		document.frmbdy.AMT.disabled=false;
		document.frmbdy.TAXAMT.disabled=false;
		document.frmbdy.CHCNT.disabled = true;
		document.frmbdy.CHCNT.value = '';
		document.all('spninmsg').innerText='';
		// document.frmbdy.btneinvoice.style.visibility = 'hidden';
		document.frmbdy.btneinvoice.setAttribute("disabled", "disabled");
		}
	else if (objchk=='3'){
		document.frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.disabled = false;
		//document.frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.value='';
		document.frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.focus();
		document.frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.style.border = 'silver 1px inset';
		document.frmbdy.YYYYMM.disabled = true;
		document.frmbdy.YYYYMM.value='';
		document.frmbdy.YYYYMM.style.border = 'none';
		document.frmbdy.UNITIVEND.disabled=true;
		document.frmbdy.UNITIVEND.value='';
		document.frmbdy.UNITIVEND.style.border = 'none';
		document.frmbdy.AMT.disabled=false;
		document.frmbdy.TAXAMT.disabled=false;
		//document.frmbdy.AMT.focus();
		document.frmbdy.CHCNT.disabled = false;
		document.all('spninmsg').innerText='(第3類單筆稅額501元以上,請逐筆登錄!)';
		// document.frmbdy.btneinvoice.style.visibility = 'hidden';
		document.frmbdy.btneinvoice.setAttribute("disabled", "disabled");
		}
	else if (objchk=='5' || objchk=='8'){
		document.frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.disabled = true;
		document.frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.value='';
		document.frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.style.border = 'none';
		document.frmbdy.YYYYMM.disabled = false;
		document.frmbdy.YYYYMM.focus();
		document.frmbdy.YYYYMM.style.border = 'silver 1px inset';
		document.frmbdy.UNITIVEND.disabled=false;
		document.frmbdy.UNITIVEND.style.border = 'silver 1px inset';
		document.frmbdy.AMT.disabled=false;
		document.frmbdy.TAXAMT.disabled=false;
		document.frmbdy.CHCNT.disabled = true;
		document.frmbdy.CHCNT.value = '';
		document.all('spninmsg').innerText='';
		// document.frmbdy.btneinvoice.style.visibility = 'hidden';
		document.frmbdy.btneinvoice.setAttribute("disabled", "disabled");
		}
	else if (objchk=='9'){ //202310 境外發票分類9
		document.frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.disabled = false;
		document.frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.focus();
		document.frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.style.border = 'silver 1px inset';
		document.frmbdy.YYYYMM.value = '';
		document.frmbdy.YYYYMM.disabled = false;
		document.frmbdy.YYYYMM.style.border = 'silver 1px inset';
		document.frmbdy.UNITIVEND.value = '';
		document.frmbdy.UNITIVEND.disabled=false;
		document.frmbdy.UNITIVEND.style.border = 'silver 1px inset';
		document.frmbdy.AMT.value = '';
		document.frmbdy.AMT.disabled=false;
		document.frmbdy.TAXAMT.value = '0';
		document.frmbdy.TAXAMT.disabled=true;
		document.frmbdy.CHCNT.disabled = true;
		document.frmbdy.CHCNT.value = '';
		document.all('spninmsg').innerText='';
		// document.frmbdy.btneinvoice.style.visibility = 'visible';
		document.frmbdy.btneinvoice.removeAttribute("disabled");
		}
	else{
		return;
		}
	}

function CHKIND_onfocus(){
	//document.all('divCHKIND').style.display='';
	var objchk=window.event.srcElement.value;
	chg_spnT(objchk);
	if (objchk=='5'){
		document.frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.value='';
		document.frmbdy.CHCNT.value = '';
		}
	}

function CHKIND_onblur(){
	var objchk=window.event.srcElement.value;
	//document.all('divCHKIND').style.display='none';
	chg_spnT(objchk);
	if (objchk=='5'){
		document.frmbdy.YYYYMM.focus();
		}
	}

function VENDUNIFORM_onkeyup() {
	var objchk=window.event.srcElement.value;
	
	if (frmbdy.CHKIND.value == '3' && objchk.length==8){
		document.frmbdy.AMT.focus();
		}
	else if (objchk.length==8){
		document.frmbdy.UNITIVEND.focus();
		//var VENDUNIFORM=frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.value;
		//alert(VENDUNIFORM);
		}	
	else{
		return;
		}
	}

function YYYYMM_onkeyup() {
	var objchk=window.event.srcElement.value;
	if (objchk.length==5){//20100928
		document.frmbdy.UNITIVEND.focus();
		}
	else if (objchk.length==4 && objchk.substring(0,2)=='99'){//20100928
		document.frmbdy.UNITIVEND.focus();
		}
	else{
		return;
		}
	}

function UNITIVEND_onkeyup() {
	var objchk=window.event.srcElement.value;
	if (objchk.length>=10 && (frmbdy.CHKIND.value =='1' || frmbdy.CHKIND.value =='2' || frmbdy.CHKIND.value =='3' || frmbdy.CHKIND.value =='6')){
		window.event.srcElement.value = objchk.substring(0,10);
		document.frmbdy.AMT.focus();
		}

	if (objchk.length>=10 && (frmbdy.CHKIND.value =='4' || frmbdy.CHKIND.value =='7')){
		window.event.srcElement.value = objchk.substring(0,10);
		document.frmbdy.AMT.focus();
		}
	
	if (objchk.length==14 && frmbdy.CHKIND.value =='5'){		
		document.frmbdy.AMT.focus();
		}
	else{
		return;
		}
	}

function AMT_onkeyup() {
	var objchk=window.event.srcElement.value;
	
	}

function DLAMT_onblur() {
	if (document.frmbdy.AMT.value==''){
		document.all('spninmsg').innerText='訊息:請輸入金額.';
		document.frmbdy.AMT.focus();
		}
	else{
		document.frmbdy.TAXAMT.focus();
		}
	}
	
function TAXAMT_onkeyup() {
	var objchk=window.event.srcElement.value;
	if (objchk.length==10){
		if (document.frmbdy.CHKIND.value=='3'){
			document.frmbdy.CHCNT.focus();
			}
		else{
			document.frmbdy.btnnew.focus();
			}
		}
	else{
		return;
		}
	}
	
function TAXAMT_onblur() {
	if (document.frmbdy.CHKIND.value=='3' && document.frmbdy.VENDUNIFORM.value==''){
		try{
			document.frmbdy.CHCNT.focus();}catch(e){}
		}
	else{
		try{
			document.frmbdy.btnnew.focus();}catch(e){}
		}
	}
	
function CHCNT_onkeyup() {
	var objchk=window.event.srcElement.value;
	if (objchk.length==4){
		try{
		document.frmbdy.btnnew.focus();}catch(e){}
		}
	else{
		return;
		}
	}

function CHCNT_onblur() {
	try{
	document.frmbdy.btnnew.focus();}catch(e){}
	}
	
//***** 檢查統編是否符合規則 *******************************************************************
function Chk_IDNO(IDNO){
	if ( IDNO.length == 8 || isNaN(parseInt(IDNO)))
	{		
		var arrIDNO = new Array();
		var i;		
		var j;
		var ChkSum=0;
		for (i=1;i<9;i++)
		{						
			arrIDNO[i]=IDNO.substring(i-1,i);	
		}
		
		var arrChk = new Array();
		arrChk[1]=1;
		arrChk[2]=2;
		arrChk[3]=1;
		arrChk[4]=2;
		arrChk[5]=1;
		arrChk[6]=2;
		arrChk[7]=4;
		arrChk[8]=1;
		
		var num1;
		var num2;
		for (i=1;i<9;i++)		
		{
			arrChk[i]=arrChk[i]*parseInt(arrIDNO[i]);
			if( arrChk[i] > 9)
			{
				num2=arrChk[i] % 10;
				num1=(arrChk[i] - num2)/10;
				arrChk[i]=num1+num2;
			}
			
			ChkSum = ChkSum + parseInt(arrChk[i]);
		}		
		num2=ChkSum % 5;		
		if ( num2 == 0 )
		{			
			return true;	
		}
		else
		{
			if(arrIDNO[7] == 7)
			{
				ChkSum=ChkSum-9;
			}
			else
			{
				ChkSum=ChkSum-1;
			}
			num2=ChkSum % 5;
			if( num2 == 0 )
			{
				return true;
			}
			else
			{	
				return false;
			}
		}
	}
	else
	{
		//window.alert('統一編號必為8位！');
		//window.parent.PSBCShop2.document.frmData.txtINDNO.focus();
		return false;
	} 
}

function btn_print(){
	if (document.frmbdy['selindata1'].length > 22){
		window.alert('列印筆數過多,按確定後,畫面資料將會轉到Excel,請調整格式後,再列印.')
		
			window.open('http://iepoch.panasonic.com.tw/FILE/FINANAPL/INPAYAPL/content/708281.CSV');
			
		}
	else{
		parent.window.print();
		}				
}

function electronic_invoice() //2023電子發票
{
    var selectElement = document.getElementById("VENDUNIFORM");
	var objchk=frmbdy.CHKIND.value; //判斷發票類別0或9
	var SELTOCOMP = parent.frames['mail'].frmbdy.SELTOCOMP.value; //取得請求付款書收件公司別 PEPH6100 2067行
	if(SELTOCOMP == '1'){
		COMP = 'T'
	}else if (SELTOCOMP == '7'){
		COMP = 'B'
	}else if (SELTOCOMP == '5'){
		COMP = 'P'
	}
	// alert(COMP);
    var selectVEND = selectElement.value;
    udl = 'PEPH6103EV.ASP?Query=0&Fr=6103&VEND='+selectVEND+'&COMP='+COMP+'&type='+objchk;
    var awindow=window.open(udl,'PEPH6103EV','height = 650px; width= 1050px; top=2px; left=2px; directories=0; scrollbars=1; location=0; resizable=1; status=1; menubar=0; titlebar=0; toolbar=0;');
    awindow.focus();
}

	}
}

function btndelF70_onclick() {
	if (intF70Sel < 0 || strF70Sobj == ''){
		document.all('spninmsgF70').innerText='請點選要刪除的一筆資料.';
		return;
		}
	for (i=0 ; i<document.frmbdy[strF70Sobj].length ; i++){
		if(document.frmbdy[strF70Sobj].options[i].selected == true){
			//alert(i);
		document.all('spninmsgF70').innerText='請點選要刪除的一筆資料.';
		return;
			}
		}
		
	if (intF70Sel < 0 || strF70Sobj == ''){
		document.all('spninmsgF70').innerText='請點選要刪除的一筆資料.';
		return;
		}
	
	//1.Update Debit Amount must equal to Total Credit Amount
	frmbdy.CFMsumF70.value = parseFloat(DeAddCommaH(frmbdy.CFMsumF70.value)) - parseFloat(frmbdy.hidCFMamt.value);
	frmbdy.CFMsumF70.value = AddCommaH(frmbdy.CFMsumF70.value);
	frmbdy.PAYsumF70.value = parseFloat(DeAddCommaH(frmbdy.PAYsumF70.value)) - parseFloat(frmbdy.hidPAYamt.value);
	frmbdy.PAYsumF70.value = AddCommaH(frmbdy.PAYsumF70.value);
	frmbdy.txtcntF70.value = parseFloat(DeAddCommaH(frmbdy.txtcntF70.value)) - 1;
	
	//3.Delete Option in Visible Select Object
	document.frmbdy[strF70Sobj].remove(intF70Sel);
	
	//6.Clear Edit Text In Input Object
	clear_F70sel();

	//7.Move Bookmark To Next If Option Exist
	if (document.frmbdy[strF70Sobj].length == 0){
		intF70Sel = -1;
		}
	else if (intF70Sel > document.frmbdy[strF70Sobj].length - 1){
		intF70Sel = -1;
		}
	else{
		document.frmbdy[strF70Sobj].options[intF70Sel].selected = true;
		selF70_gv(strF70Sobj);
		}
		
	//8.Show Msg
	parent.frames['FIND'].location.href = 'peph6102.asp?action=F70del';
}

function btnnewF70_onclick(DOCN,trncard) {
	if (chk_F70_v('a') == false){
		return false;
		}
	document.all('spninmsgF70').innerText='訊息:檢查中,請稍後..';
	document.all('errmsg1').innerText='';
	
	strF70Sobj = 'selF70cfm1';
	re = /\xA0/g;
	for(dupi=0;dupi<document.frmbdy[strF70Sobj].length;dupi++){
		ss = document.frmbdy[strF70Sobj].options[dupi].text.split(';')
		if (ss.length < 3) break			
		ss[0] = ss[0].replace(re,"");
		ss[1] = ss[1].replace(re,"");
		
		if (trim(ss[0]) + ss[1] == frmbdy.CFMNO.value + frmbdy.USEDEPT.value){
			document.all('spninmsgF70').innerText='';
			strF70Sobj = '';
			window.alert('此筆重複輸入!') 
			return false;
			}
		}	
		
	//Check All Doc
	strURL = 'peph6102.asp?action=F70add&intSel=' + intF70Sel + '&sel=' + strF70Sobj
	strURL = strURL + '&ck=' + frmbdy.CFMNO.value;
	strURL = strURL + '&cm=' + DeAddCommaH(frmbdy.CFMAMT.value);
	strURL = strURL + '&pm=' + DeAddCommaH(frmbdy.PAYAMT.value);
	strURL = strURL + '&cu=' + frmbdy.USEDEPT.value;
	
	try{bugarea=parent.frames['mail'].frmbdy.SELTOCOMP.value;}
		catch(e){bugarea='1';}
	strURL = strURL + '&bugarea=' + bugarea;
	try{strURL = strURL + '&txtmon2=' + frmbdy.txtmon2.value;}
		catch(e){}
		
	strURL = strURL + '&dt=' + TimeDemo();
	parent.frames['FIND'].location.href = strURL;
}

//Check In-Value
function chk_F70_v(act) {
	if (frmbdy.CFMNO.value.length != 9){
		document.all('spninmsgF70').innerText='訊息:編號輸入錯誤!';
		frmbdy.CFMNO.focus();
		return false;}
	if (frmbdy.USEDEPT.value.length != 3){
		document.all('spninmsgF70').innerText='訊息:單位輸入錯誤!';
		frmbdy.USEDEPT.focus();
		return false;}
	if (frmbdy.CFMAMT.value == '' || frmbdy.PAYAMT.value == '' || frmbdy.CFMAMT.value == '0' || frmbdy.PAYAMT.value == '0'){
		document.all('spninmsgF70').innerText='訊息:金額輸入錯誤!';
		frmbdy.CFMAMT.focus();
		return false;}
	return true;
}

var intF70Sel
var strF70Sobj
//Select object
function selF70cfm_onclick(evtobj,strmd,strcf,strSt) {
	if (((strmd == '99' || strmd == '97') && strcf != 'Y') || (strSt != 'B' && strSt != 'C')){
		currentTab = evtobj; //window.event.srcElement;
		//功能列按鈕id
		if (typeof(currentTab) != "object" || currentTab == null)//IE ERR
		{
			return;
		}
		if (typeof(currentTab.id) == 'undefined' )//CHROME ERR
		{
			return;
		}
		//alert(currentTab.selectedIndex);

		try{intF70Sel = currentTab.selectedIndex;}catch(e){}
		if (intF70Sel >= 0) selF70_gv(currentTab.id);
		}
	else{
		event.srcElement.selectedIndex = -1;
		}
	}

function selF70_gv(selid) {
	s  = document.frmbdy[selid].options[intF70Sel].text;	
	document.frmbdy[selid].selectedIndex = -1;
	if (s.indexOf(';') > 0){
		ss = s.split(';');
		re = /\xA0/g;
		ss[0] = ss[0].replace(re,"");
		ss[1] = ss[1].replace(re,"");
		ss[2] = ss[2].replace(re,"");
		ss[3] = ss[3].replace(re,"");
		
		frmbdy.CFMNO.value		 = ss[0];
		frmbdy.USEDEPT.value	 = trim(ss[1]);
		frmbdy.CFMAMT.value		 = parseFloat(ss[2]);
		frmbdy.PAYAMT.value		 = parseFloat(ss[3]);

		frmbdy.hidCFMamt.value	 = parseFloat(ss[2]);
		frmbdy.hidPAYamt.value	 = parseFloat(ss[3]);
			
		strF70Sobj = selid;
		document.all("spninmsgF70").innerText = "";
		document.frmbdy.btnupdF70.disabled = false;
		document.frmbdy.btndelF70.disabled = false;
		document.frmbdy.btnnewF70.disabled = true;
		}
	else{
		clear_F70sel();
		strF70Sobj = '';
		intF70Sel = - 1;
		}
	}

function clear_F70sel() {
	frmbdy.CFMNO.value		 = '';
	frmbdy.CFMAMT.value = '';
	frmbdy.PAYAMT.value		 = '';
	frmbdy.USEDEPT.value	 = '';
	document.frmbdy.btnupdF70.disabled = true;
	document.frmbdy.btndelF70.disabled = true;
	document.frmbdy.btnnewF70.disabled = false;
	}

function PAYAMT_onblur() {

		return;
		}
	else if (parseInt(frmbdy.PAYAMT.value,10)/1 != frmbdy.PAYAMT.value || parseFloat(frmbdy.PAYAMT.value) <= 0){
		document.all('spninmsgF70').innerText='訊息:金額請輸入整數!';
		document.frmbdy.PAYAMT.value='';
		document.frmbdy.PAYAMT.focus();
		return ;
		}		
	else{
		document.all('spninmsgF70').innerText='';
		}
	}

function btnPrF80_onclick() {
	document.all('spninmsgF80').style.display = 'none';
	frmbdy.btnTVHF80.style.display = 'none';
	frmbdy.btnSNOF80.style.display = 'none';
	frmbdy.btnFGNF80.style.display = 'none';
	frmbdy.btnF80GET.style.display = 'none';
	frmbdy.btnPrF80.style.display = 'none';
	window.print();
	btnPrF80_onafterprint();
}

function btnPrF80_onafterprint() {
	document.all('spninmsgF80').style.display = '';	
	frmbdy.btnTVHF80.style.display = '';
	frmbdy.btnSNOF80.style.display = '';
	frmbdy.btnFGNF80.style.display = '';
	frmbdy.btnF80GET.style.display = '';
	frmbdy.btnPrF80.style.display = '';
}

function PBUGNOF80_onblur() {
	if (document.frmbdy.onbluecntF80.value=='Y'){
		document.frmbdy.PMEMONOF80.focus();
		return;
		}
	document.frmbdy.onbluecntF80.value='Y';	
	if (document.frmbdy.PBUGNOF80.value==''){
		document.frmbdy.HPBUGNOF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.onbluecntF80.value='';
		return;
		}
	var chk=document.frmbdy.PBUGNOF80.value;
	if 	(chk.substring(0,1)==' '){
		document.frmbdy.PBUGNOF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.HPBUGNOF80.value='';
		alert('預算單位不可空白');
		document.frmbdy.PBUGNOF80.focus();
		document.frmbdy.onbluecntF80.value='';
		return;
		}	
		
	var bugvno=document.frmbdy.PBUGNOF80.value;
	bugvno=bugvno.toUpperCase();
	document.frmbdy.PBUGNOF80.value=bugvno;
	parent.frames['FIND'].location.href = 'PEPH6082.asp?ACTION=buggetF80&BUGVNO=' + bugvno + '&bugarea=' + document.frmbdy.SELTOCOMP.value +'&T='+'20260126113634';
}

function PCREADF80_onblur() {
	var chk=document.frmbdy.PCREADF80.value;
	if 	(chk.substring(0,1)==''){
		return;
		}	
	if 	(chk.substring(0,1)==' '){
		document.frmbdy.PCREADF80.value='';
		return;
		}	
	if (isNaN(parseInt(document.frmbdy.PCREADF80.value))){
		alert('金額請輸入數字');
		document.frmbdy.PCREADF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.PCREADF80.focus();
		return;
		}	
	if (parseInt(document.frmbdy.PCREADF80.value,10)==0){
		alert('金額不可為零或空白');
		document.frmbdy.PCREADF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.PCREADF80.focus();
		return;
		}
	if (trncard == '002') {
		document.frmbdy.PCREADF80.value=Math.round(parseFloat(document.frmbdy.PCREADF80.value)*100)/100;
		}
	else{
		document.frmbdy.PCREADF80.value=Math.round(parseInt(document.frmbdy.PCREADF80.value,10));
		}
}

	document.frmbdy.PCFMNOF80.focus();
}

		}
	else{
		return;

function PCFMNOF80_onblur() {
	var chk=document.frmbdy.PCFMNOF80.value;
	if 	(chk.substring(0,1)==''){
		document.frmbdy.HPCFMNOF80.value='';
		return;
		}	
	if 	(chk.substring(0,1)==' '){
		document.frmbdy.PCFMNOF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.HPCFMNOF80.value='';
		return;
		}

	document.frmbdy.PCFMNOF80.value=chk.toUpperCase();
	document.frmbdy.HPCFMNOF80.value=chk.toUpperCase();
	return;
}

//資料新增一筆
function ADDF80_onclick() {
	if (document.frmbdy.onbluecntF80.value=='Y'){
		return;
		}
	if(document.frmbdy.oRowcntF80.value=='18' && document.frmbdy.oSpacntF80.value=='0'){
		alert('資料筆數不可超過18筆');
		return;
		}
	if(document.frmbdy.PTSNOF80.value=='' || document.frmbdy.PTSNOF80.value.substring(0,1)==' '){
		alert('序號不可空白');
		return;
		}
	if(document.frmbdy.POBJNOF80.value=='' || document.frmbdy.POBJNOF80.value.substring(0,1)==' '){
		alert('科目不可空白');
		return;
		}
	if(document.frmbdy.PBUGNOF80.value=='' || document.frmbdy.PBUGNOF80.value.substring(0,1)==' '){
		alert('單位不可空白');
		return;
		}	
	if(document.frmbdy.PCREADF80.value=='' || document.frmbdy.PCREADF80.value=='0'){
		alert('金額不可空白');
		return;
		}		
	if(document.frmbdy.PCREADF80.value.length > 11){
		alert('金額位數超過');
		return;
		}		
	if (document.frmbdy.POBJNAMEF80.value==''){
			alert('科目名稱空白，請確認科目');
			return;
		}		
	if(document.frmbdy.POBJNOF80.value!=document.frmbdy.HPOBJNOF80.value){
		return;
		}
	if(document.frmbdy.PITEMNOF80.value!=document.frmbdy.HPITEMNOF80.value){
		return;
		}
	if(document.frmbdy.PMEMONOF80.value!=document.frmbdy.HPMEMONOF80.value){
		return;
		}		
	if(document.frmbdy.PBUGNOF80.value!=document.frmbdy.HPBUGNOF80.value){
		return;
		}			
	if (document.frmbdy.PCFMNOF80.value!=document.frmbdy.HPCFMNOF80.value){			
		return;
		}	
		    						
	tsnoin=document.frmbdy.PTSNOF80.value;		    						
	objin=document.frmbdy.POBJNOF80.value;
	itemin=document.frmbdy.PITEMNOF80.value;
	bugin=document.frmbdy.PBUGNOF80.value;
	menoin=document.frmbdy.PMEMONOF80.value;
	paydocin=document.frmbdy.PAPLYRSNF80.value;
	objnamein=document.frmbdy.POBJNAMEF80.value;
	compno=document.frmbdy.PCFMTYPEF80.value;
	invoin=document.frmbdy.PCFMNOF80.value;
	creadin=document.frmbdy.PCREADF80.value;
	if (Math.abs(document.frmbdy.oSpacntF80.value) > 0 ){
		//Update
		rowcnt = Math.abs(document.frmbdy.oRowcntF80.value) - Math.abs(document.frmbdy.oSpacntF80.value);
		addcnt = parseInt(document.form2.selRowF80.options[rowcnt].value) ;
		oAddRowF80_onclick('U', rowcnt, addcnt,tsnoin,objin,itemin,bugin,menoin,paydocin,objnamein,invoin,compno,creadin);
		}
	else{
		//Insert 	
		rowcnt = Math.abs(document.frmbdy.oRowcntF80.value);
		addcnt = Math.abs(document.frmbdy.oAddcntF80.value)
		oAddRowF80_onclick('A',rowcnt, addcnt,tsnoin,objin,itemin,bugin,menoin,paydocin,objnamein,invoin,compno,creadin);
		}

	document.frmbdy.PTSNOF80.focus();

	document.frmbdy.CorindF80.value='';
	document.frmbdy.PTSNOF80.value='';	
	document.frmbdy.POBJNOF80.value='';
	document.frmbdy.PITEMNOF80.value='';
	document.frmbdy.PBUGNOF80.value='';
	document.frmbdy.PMEMONOF80.value='';
	document.frmbdy.PAPLYRSNF80.value='';
	document.frmbdy.POBJNAMEF80.value='';
	document.frmbdy.PCFMTYPEF80.value='';
	document.frmbdy.PCFMNOF80.value='';
	//隱藏欄位
	document.frmbdy.HPOBJNOF80.value='';
	document.frmbdy.HPITEMNOF80.value='';
	document.frmbdy.HPBUGNOF80.value='';
	document.frmbdy.HPMEMONOF80.value='';
	document.frmbdy.HPCFMTYPEF80.value='';
	document.frmbdy.HPCFMNOF80.value='';
	//***********************
	document.frmbdy.PCREADF80.value='';
	document.frmbdy.ADDF80.disabled=false;
	document.frmbdy.UPDF80.disabled=true;
	document.frmbdy.DELF80.disabled=true;
}

//已輸入資料更正 將資料取出至更正位置
function CORF80_onclick(A1) {
	if(document.all['OBJNO'+A1+'_F80'].value!='' || document.all['OBJNAME'+A1+'_F80'].value!=''){
		document.frmbdy.PTSNOF80.value=document.all['TSNO'+A1+'_F80'].value;
		document.frmbdy.POBJNOF80.value=document.all['OBJNO'+A1+'_F80'].value;
		document.frmbdy.PITEMNOF80.value=document.all['ITEMNO'+A1+'_F80'].value;
		document.frmbdy.PBUGNOF80.value=document.all['BUGNO'+A1+'_F80'].value;
		document.frmbdy.PMEMONOF80.value=document.all['MEMONO'+A1+'_F80'].value;
		document.frmbdy.HPOBJNOF80.value=document.all['OBJNO'+A1+'_F80'].value;
		document.frmbdy.HPITEMNOF80.value=document.all['ITEMNO'+A1+'_F80'].value;
		document.frmbdy.HPBUGNOF80.value=document.all['BUGNO'+A1+'_F80'].value;
		document.frmbdy.HPMEMONOF80.value=document.all['MEMONO'+A1+'_F80'].value;
		document.frmbdy.PAPLYRSNF80.value=document.all['APLYRSNU'+A1+'_F80'].value+document.all['APLYRSNL'+A1+'_F80'].value;
	
			
		if (trncard == '002') {
			document.frmbdy.PAPLYRSNF80.value=document.all['APLYRSNU'+A1+'_F80'].value;
			}
	
		
		document.frmbdy.POBJNAMEF80.value=document.all['OBJNAME'+A1+'_F80'].value;
		document.frmbdy.PCFMTYPEF80.value=document.all['CFMTYPE'+A1+'_F80'].value;
		document.frmbdy.PCFMNOF80.value=document.all['CFMNO'+A1+'_F80'].value;
		document.frmbdy.HPCFMTYPEF80.value=document.all['CFMTYPE'+A1+'_F80'].value;
		document.frmbdy.HPCFMNOF80.value=document.all['CFMNO'+A1+'_F80'].value;
		document.frmbdy.PCREADF80.value=document.all['CREAD'+A1+'_F80'].value;
		
		document.frmbdy.DELF80.disabled=false;	
		document.frmbdy.ADDF80.disabled=false;
		document.frmbdy.UPDF80.disabled=false;
		document.frmbdy.CorindF80.value=A1;	
		document.frmbdy.PTSNOF80.focus();		
		}
}
//已輸入資料更新
function UPDF80_onclick() {
	if (document.frmbdy.onbluecntF80.value=='Y'){
		return;
		}
	if(document.frmbdy.PTSNOF80.value=='' || document.frmbdy.PTSNOF80.value.substring(0,1)==' '){
		alert('序號不可空白');
		return;
		}
	if(document.frmbdy.POBJNOF80.value=='' || document.frmbdy.POBJNOF80.value.substring(0,1)==' '){
		alert('科目不可空白');
		return;
		}
	if(document.frmbdy.PBUGNOF80.value=='' || document.frmbdy.PBUGNOF80.value.substring(0,1)==' '){
		alert('單位不可空白');
		return;
		}	
	if(document.frmbdy.PCREADF80.value=='' || document.frmbdy.PCREADF80.value=='0'){
		alert('金額不可空白');
		return;
		}				
	if(document.frmbdy.PCREADF80.value.length > 11){
		alert('金額位數超過');
		return;
		}
	if (document.frmbdy.POBJNAMEF80.value==''){
		alert('科目名稱空白，請確認科目');
		return;
		}
	if(document.frmbdy.POBJNOF80.value!=document.frmbdy.HPOBJNOF80.value){
		return;
		}
	if(document.frmbdy.PITEMNOF80.value!=document.frmbdy.HPITEMNOF80.value){
		return;
		}
	if(document.frmbdy.PMEMONOF80.value!=document.frmbdy.HPMEMONOF80.value){
		return;
		}		
	if(document.frmbdy.PBUGNOF80.value!=document.frmbdy.HPBUGNOF80.value){
		return;
		}			
	if (document.frmbdy.PCFMNOF80.value!=document.frmbdy.HPCFMNOF80.value){			
			return;
			}		
	var A1=document.frmbdy.CorindF80.value;
	if (A1!=''){
		document.all['TSNO'+A1+'_F80'].value=document.frmbdy.PTSNOF80.value;
		document.all['OBJNO'+A1+'_F80'].value=document.frmbdy.POBJNOF80.value;
		document.all['ITEMNO'+A1+'_F80'].value=document.frmbdy.PITEMNOF80.value;
		document.all['BUGNO'+A1+'_F80'].value=document.frmbdy.PBUGNOF80.value;
		document.all['MEMONO'+A1+'_F80'].value=document.frmbdy.PMEMONOF80.value;
		document.all['APLYRSNU'+A1+'_F80'].value = BSubstr(document.frmbdy.PAPLYRSNF80.value,0,20)
		 
		if (trncard != '002') {
			document.all['APLYRSNL'+A1+'_F80'].value = BSubstr(document.frmbdy.PAPLYRSNF80.value,20,40);		
			}
		else{
	
			}
			
		document.frmbdy.PTSNOF80.focus();

		document.all['OBJNAME'+A1+'_F80'].value=document.frmbdy.POBJNAMEF80.value;
		document.all['CFMTYPE'+A1+'_F80'].value=document.frmbdy.PCFMTYPEF80.value;
		document.all['CFMNO'+A1+'_F80'].value=document.frmbdy.PCFMNOF80.value;
		document.all['CREAD'+A1+'_F80'].value=document.frmbdy.PCREADF80.value;
		document.all['Desc' +A1+'_F80'].value='';
		
		if ((trncard == '002' || trncard == 'N07')){
			document.all['CREADV'+A1+'_F80'].value = AddCommaH(document.all['CREAD'+A1+'_F80'].value);
			}
		else{
			document.all['CREADV'+A1+'_F80'].value = AddComma(document.all['CREAD'+A1+'_F80'].value);
			}
		document.frmbdy.CorindF80.value='';	
		document.frmbdy.PTSNOF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.POBJNOF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.PITEMNOF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.PBUGNOF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.PMEMONOF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.PAPLYRSNF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.POBJNAMEF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.PCFMTYPEF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.PCFMNOF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.HPOBJNOF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.HPITEMNOF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.HPBUGNOF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.HPMEMONOF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.HPCFMTYPEF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.HPCFMNOF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.PCREADF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.ADDF80.disabled=false;
		oSumF80_onclick();				
		document.frmbdy.UPDF80.disabled=true;
		document.frmbdy.DELF80.disabled=true;		
		}
}
//資料刪除
function DELF80_onclick() {
	if (document.frmbdy.onbluecntF80.value=='Y'){
		return;
		}	
	var A1=document.frmbdy.CorindF80.value;
    if (A1!=''){
		var rowcount=parseInt(document.frmbdy.oRowcntF80.value);
		for (var icount1 = 1; icount1< rowcount+1; icount1++)
			{
			if (document.form2.selRowF80.options[icount1-1].value==A1)
				{
				dd=icount1;
				break;
				}
			}
		j = document.form2.selRowF80.options[dd-1].value;
		var temp = 'CREAD';
		temp = temp +A1+'_F80';
		document.frmbdy.oRowcntF80.value = document.frmbdy.oRowcntF80.value - 1;
		otblF80.deleteRow(dd);    
		document.form2.selRowF80.remove(dd-1);
		if (Math.abs(document.frmbdy.oRowcntF80.value) < 18){
			document.frmbdy.oSpacntF80.value = Math.abs(document.frmbdy.oSpacntF80.value) + 1;
			oAddRowF80_onclick('A',document.frmbdy.oRowcntF80.value, document.frmbdy.oAddcntF80.value,'','','','','','','','','','');	
			}
		oSumF80_onclick();			

		document.frmbdy.CorindF80.value='';	
		document.frmbdy.PTSNOF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.POBJNOF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.PITEMNOF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.PBUGNOF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.PMEMONOF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.PAPLYRSNF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.POBJNAMEF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.PCFMTYPEF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.PCFMNOF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.HPOBJNOF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.HPITEMNOF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.HPBUGNOF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.HPMEMONOF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.HPCFMTYPEF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.HPCFMNOF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.PCREADF80.value='';
		document.frmbdy.ADDF80.disabled=false;
		document.frmbdy.UPDF80.disabled=true;	
		document.frmbdy.DELF80.disabled=true;
		}
}
//增加,維護一列
function oAddRowF80_onclick(strcd,rowcnt,addcnt,tsnoin,objin,itemin,bugin,menoin,paydocin,objnamein,invoin,compno,creadin) {
	rowcnt = parseInt(rowcnt) + 1;
	addcnt = parseInt(addcnt) + 1;
	var addcnt1 = addcnt-1 ;
	if (strcd == 'A'){
		otblF80.insertRow(rowcnt);
		document.frmbdy.oAddcntF80.value = Math.abs(document.frmbdy.oAddcntF80.value) + 1;
		document.frmbdy.oRowcntF80.value = Math.abs(document.frmbdy.oRowcntF80.value) + 1;
		var aElement = document.createElement('option');
		aElement.value = addcnt;
		aElement.text = addcnt;    
		document.form2.selRowF80.options.add(aElement);	
		}
	else if (strcd == 'U'){
		otblF80.deleteRow(rowcnt);
		otblF80.insertRow(rowcnt);
		document.frmbdy.oSpacntF80.value = Math.abs(document.frmbdy.oSpacntF80.value) - 1;
		}	
	for (i=0;i<6;i++){
	otblF80.rows[rowcnt].insertCell();
	}
	
		var aclick='';	
		
	
	otblF80.rows[rowcnt].cells[0].width=200;
	var a='<TABLE BORDER=0  cellPadding="0" cellSpacing="0" ' + aclick + '  WIDTH=100%><tr>';
	a=a + '<TD COLSPAN=3  align=center style="border:thin solid silver;border-top:none;border-left:none;border-right:none;">';
	a=a + '<INPUT type="text" id=OBJNAME'+addcnt1+'_F80' + ' name=OBJNAME'+addcnt1+'_F80' + ' size=22 value="' + objnamein + '" style="border:none;text-align: left;font-size:14px" readonly>';
	a=a + '</TD></TR><TR>';
	
	a=a + '<TD align=center style="width:40;border:thin solid silver;border-top:none;border-bottom:none;border-left:none;">';
	a=a + '<INPUT type="text" id=TSNO'+addcnt1+'_F80'+ ' name=TSNO'+addcnt1+'_F80'+ '  value="' + tsnoin + '" style="width:100%;border:none;text-align:center;font-size:16px" readonly>';

	a=a + '<TD align=center style="width:100px;border:thin solid silver;border-top:none;border-bottom:none;border-left:none;">';
	a=a + '<INPUT type="text" id=OBJNO'+addcnt1+'_F80' + ' name=OBJNO'+addcnt1+'_F80' + '  value="' + objin + '" style="width:100%;border:none;text-align:center;font-size:16px" readonly>';

	a=a + '</TD><TD align=center style="width:60px;border:thin solid silver;border-top:none;border-bottom:none;border-left:none;border-right:none;">';
	a=a + '<INPUT type="text" id=ITEMNO'+addcnt1+'_F80' + ' name=ITEMNO'+addcnt1+'_F80' + '   value="' + itemin + '" style="width:100%;border:none;text-align:center;font-size:16px" readonly>';	
	a=a + '</TD></TR></TABLE>';
	otblF80.rows[rowcnt].cells[0].insertAdjacentHTML('beforeEnd',a);
	
	otblF80.rows[rowcnt].cells[1].width=45;
	var b= '<TABLE BORDER=0 cellPadding="0" cellSpacing="0" ' + aclick + ' WIDTH=100%><TR>';
	b=b + '<TD align=center style="border:thin solid silver;border-top:none;border-left:none;border-right:none;">';
	b=b + '<INPUT type="text" id=MEMONO'+addcnt1+'_F80' + ' name=MEMONO'+addcnt1+'_F80' + ' value="' + menoin + '" style="width:100%;border:none;text-align: center;font-size:16px" readonly>';
	b=b + '</TD></TR><TR>';
	
	b=b + '<TD align=center style="border:thin solid silver;border-top:none;border-bottom:none;border-left:none;border-right:none;">';
	b=b + '<INPUT type="text" id=BUGNO'+addcnt1+'_F80' + ' name=BUGNO'+addcnt1+'_F80' + ' value="' + bugin + '" style="width:100%;border:none;text-align: center;font-size:16px" readonly>';
	b=b + '</TD></TR></TABLE>';
	otblF80.rows[rowcnt].cells[1].insertAdjacentHTML('beforeEnd',b);
	
	otblF80.rows[rowcnt].cells[2].width=120;
	var c='<INPUT type="text" id=CREADV'+addcnt1+'_F80'+ ' name=CREADV'+addcnt1+'_F80' + ' value="" style="width:100%;border:none;text-align: right;font-size:16px" readonly>';
	c=c + '<INPUT type="HIDDEN" id=CREAD' + addcnt1 +'_F80' + ' name=CREAD' + addcnt1 +'_F80' + ' value="' + creadin + '" style="border:none;text-align: right;font-size:16px" readonly>';
	otblF80.rows[rowcnt].cells[2].insertAdjacentHTML('beforeEnd',c);	
	//alert(document.all['CREAD'+addcnt1+'_F80'].value);
	if ((trncard == '002' || trncard == 'N07') && document.all['CREAD'+addcnt1+'_F80'].value != ''){
		document.all['CREADV'+addcnt1+'_F80'].value = AddCommaH(document.all['CREAD'+addcnt1+'_F80'].value);
		}
	else
		{
		document.all['CREADV'+addcnt1+'_F80'].value = AddComma(document.all['CREAD'+addcnt1+'_F80'].value);
		}
	
	otblF80.rows[rowcnt].cells[3].width=150;
	var d='<TABLE BORDER=0 cellPadding="0" cellSpacing="0" ' + aclick + ' WIDTH=100%><TR>';
	d=d + '<TD align=center style="border:thin solid silver;border-top:none;border-left:none;border-right:none;">';
	d=d + '<INPUT type="text" id=CFMTYPE'+addcnt1+'_F80' + ' name=CFMTYPE'+addcnt1+'_F80' + ' size=10 value="' + compno + '" style="border:none;text-align: left;font-size:16px" readonly>';

	d=d + '</TD></TR><TR><TD align=center style="">';
	d=d + '<INPUT type="text" id=CFMNO'+addcnt1+'_F80' + ' name=CFMNO'+addcnt1+'_F80' + ' size=10 value="' + invoin + '" style="border:none;text-align: leftt;font-size:16px" readonly>';
	d=d + '</TD></TR></TABLE>';
	otblF80.rows[rowcnt].cells[3].insertAdjacentHTML('beforeEnd',d);	
	
	otblF80.rows[rowcnt].cells[4].width=170;
	var e='<TABLE BORDER=0 cellPadding="0" cellSpacing="0" ' + aclick + ' width=100%><TR>';
	e=e + '<TD style="">';
	e=e + '<INPUT type="text" id=APLYRSNU'+addcnt1+'_F80' + ' name=APLYRSNU'+addcnt1+'_F80' + ' size=20 value="' + BSubstr(paydocin,0,20) + '" style="border:none;text-align:left;font-size:14px" readonly>';
	//e=e + '<INPUT type="text" id=APLYRSNU'+addcnt1+'_F80' + ' name=APLYRSNU'+addcnt1+'_F80' + ' size=20 value="' + paydocin.substring(0,10) + '" style="border:none;text-align:left;font-size:14px" readonly>';
	
	e=e + '</TD></TR><TR>';
	e=e + '<TD style="">';
	e=e + '<INPUT type="text" id=APLYRSNL'+addcnt1+'_F80' + ' name=APLYRSNL'+addcnt1+'_F80' + ' size=20 value="' + BSubstr(paydocin,20,40) + '" style="border:none;text-align:left;font-size:14px" readonly>';
	//e=e + '<INPUT type="text" id=APLYRSNL'+addcnt1+'_F80' + ' name=APLYRSNL'+addcnt1+'_F80' + ' size=20 value="' + paydocin.substring(10,20) + '" style="border:none;text-align:left;font-size:14px" readonly>';
	e=e + '</TD></TR></TABLE>';
	otblF80.rows[rowcnt].cells[4].insertAdjacentHTML('beforeEnd',e);	
	
	
	
	oSumF80_onclick();
	
}

//選決裁書
function btnSNOF80_onclick(s,CFMtype) {
	var ACTNO="";
	var ACTITEM="";
	var ACTBUG="";
	if (s =="S"){
		if (document.frmbdy.PCFMTYPEF80.value == ""){
			alert("請選擇決裁書分類");
			document.frmbdy.PCFMTYPEF80.focus();
			return;
			}
		else {
			CFMtype = document.frmbdy.PCFMTYPEF80.value;
			}
		if (document.frmbdy.POBJNOF80.value == ""){
			alert("請選擇傳票參照");
			document.frmbdy.POBJNOF80.focus();
			return;
			}
		else {
			ACTNO = document.frmbdy.POBJNOF80.value;
			ACTITEM = document.frmbdy.PITEMNOF80.value;
			ACTBUG = document.frmbdy.PBUGNOF80.value;
			}

		}
	document.all("btnSNOF80").style.color="silver";
	document.all("btnSNOF80").disabled=true;			
	document.all("btnTVHF80").style.color="silver";
	document.all("btnTVHF80").disabled=true;			
	document.all("btnFGNF80").style.color="silver";
	document.all("btnFGNF80").disabled=true;			
	document.all("btnF80GET").style.color="silver";
	document.all("btnF80GET").disabled=true;	
	document.all("btnPrF80").style.color="silver";
	document.all("btnPrF80").disabled=true;	

	var a			= document.createElement("div");
	a.name			= "CFMDispdialogue";
	a.id			= "CFMDispdialogue";
	a.style.position= "absolute";
	a.style.width	= "750px";
	a.style.height	= "400px";
	
	a.style.left	= "100px";
	a.style.left	= parseInt((screen.availWidth/2)-(parseInt(a.style.width,10)/2),10)-15;
	a.style.top		= "200px";
	//a.style.top		= parseInt((screen.availHeight/2)-(parseInt(a.style.height,10)/2),10)+40;
	a.style.border	= "3px solid PaleTurquoise";
	a.style.backgroundColor	= "Moccasin";
	a.style.visibility= "visible";
	document.frmbdy.appendChild(a);
	//window.alert("x");

	var b			= document.createElement("iframe");
	b.name			= "CFMDispiframe";
	b.id			= "CFMDispiframe";
	b.style.width	= parseInt(a.style.width,10)-10;
	b.style.height	= parseInt(a.style.height,10)-10;
	b.align	= "left"
	b.frameBorder 	= 0;
	//alert(trncard);
	if (trncard == '002') {
		b.src = "peph6081.asp?btn=" + s + "&CFMtype=" + CFMtype + "&ACTNO=" + ACTNO + "&ACTITEM=" + ACTITEM + "&ACTBUG=" + ACTBUG +'&BUGAREA='+parent.frames['mail'].frmbdy.SELTOCOMP.value +'&CUCY='+parent.frames['mail'].frmbdy.hdCUCY.value + "&time=" + TimeDemo();
		}
	else{
		b.src = "peph6081.asp?btn=" + s + "&CFMtype=" + CFMtype + "&ACTNO=" + ACTNO + "&ACTITEM=" + ACTITEM + "&ACTBUG=" + ACTBUG +'&BUGAREA='+parent.frames['mail'].frmbdy.SELTOCOMP.value + "&time=" + TimeDemo();
		}	
	//b.src = "peph6081.asp?btn=" + s + "&CFMtype=" + CFMtype + "&ACTNO=" + ACTNO + "&ACTITEM=" + ACTITEM + "&ACTBUG=" + ACTBUG +'&BUGAREA='+parent.frames['mail'].frmbdy.SELTOCOMP.value +'&CUCY='+parent.frames['mail'].frmbdy.hdCUCY.value + "&time=" + TimeDemo();
	a.appendChild(b);
	var obj = document.getElementById('CFMDispdialogue');	
	rDrag.init(obj);
	return;
}

//填入通用編號
function btnFGNF80_onclick(){
	if (document.frmbdy.PCFMTYPEF80.value == ""){
		alert("請選擇決裁書分類");
		document.frmbdy.PCFMTYPEF80.focus();
		return;
	}
	
	var PCFMTYPEF80 = document.frmbdy.PCFMTYPEF80.value;
	var PCFMNOF80 = "9999999999";
	document.frmbdy.PCFMTYPEF80.value = PCFMTYPEF80;
	document.frmbdy.PCFMNOF80.value = PCFMNOF80;
	document.frmbdy.PCFMNOF80.focus();
	PCFMNOF80_onkeyup();	
	
	for (i=0;i<18-document.frmbdy.oSpacntF80.value;i++){
		if ( document.getElementById('CREADV'+i+'_F80').value != 0 && document.getElementById('CFMNO'+i+'_F80').value==""){
			document.getElementById('CFMNO'+i+'_F80').value= PCFMNOF80;
			}
		if ( document.getElementById('CREADV'+i+'_F80').value != 0 && document.getElementById('CFMTYPE'+i+'_F80').value==""){
			document.getElementById('CFMTYPE'+i+'_F80').value= PCFMTYPEF80;
			}
		}
}	
//共用:各明細區按儲存文件後,轉回原明細區
function btnSAVF80_onclick(){
	if (document.all("btnsave").disabled==false){
		document.all("btnsave").click();
	}
}

//共用:明細區按開啟文件
function CFMNO_F80_onclick(s1,s2){
	//window.alert(doc_src);
	//return;
	var doc_src = "";
	doc_src		= "peph6084.asp?time="+TimeDemo()+"&s1="+s1+"&s2="+s2;
	if (s1 >="B01" && s2 !="" && s2 != "9999999999"){

		var a			= document.createElement("div");
		a.name			= "CFMDispdialogue";
		a.id			= "CFMDispdialogue";
		a.style.position= "absolute";
		a.style.width	= screen.availWidth;
		//a.style.height	= "400px";	//20200616
		a.style.height	= "850px";		//20200707
	
		a.style.left	= "300px";
		a.style.left	= parseInt((screen.availWidth/2)-(parseInt(a.style.width,10)/2),10)-15;
		a.style.top		= "150px";	//20200707
		//a.style.top		= parseInt((screen.availHeight/2)-(parseInt(a.style.height,10)/2),10)+40;
		a.style.border	= "3px solid PaleTurquoise";
		a.style.backgroundColor	= "Moccasin";
		a.style.visibility= "visible";
		document.frmbdy.appendChild(a);
		//window.alert("x");

		var b			= document.createElement("iframe");
		b.name			= "CFMDispiframe";
		b.id			= "CFMDispiframe";
		b.style.width	= parseInt(a.style.width,10)-10;
		b.style.height	= parseInt(a.style.height,10)-10;
		b.align			= "left";
		b.frameBorder 	= 0;
		b.src			= doc_src;
		a.appendChild(b);
		var obj = document.getElementById('CFMDispdialogue');	
		rDrag.init(obj);		
	}
	
}
